class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}$</math-renderer> 之后认为这是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r^{1/2}$</math-renderer>……</li>\n</ol>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-二运算步骤相关\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x,y,z) = 0$</math-renderer> 给了 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0,y_0$</math-renderer>，让求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$dz \\vert (x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">结果我就只想着把 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 代入算出的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$dz$</math-renderer>，式中的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$z$</math-renderer> 变量居然被我保留了，我居然没有把 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x,y,z) = 0$</math-renderer> 去算 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$z_0$</math-renderer>……</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">算得了一个复杂的式子，可以暂时用一个符号来代替他</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">原理是，在计算的时候只需要知道这个复杂的式子的某个性质，而不需要具体计算</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y(x)$</math-renderer> 满足 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y'' + 2ay' + b^2y = 0,a&amp;gt;b&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer>，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y(0)=1,y'(0) = 1$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^{+\\infty}{y(x)dx} =$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这题可以计算出微分方程的两个特征根的解析式，但是只需要把解写成 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = c_1e^{r_1x} + c_2e^{r_2x}$</math-renderer> 就好了</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因为只需要知道 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r_1,r_2 &amp;lt; 0$</math-renderer>，算 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^{+\\infty}{y(x)dx}$</math-renderer> 时是把题目条件代入，得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^{+\\infty}{-\\dfrac{1}{b^2}(y'' + 2ay')dx}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-三逻辑相关\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#三逻辑相关\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" href=\"#11-证明-xxx-唯一\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.1 证明 XXX 唯一</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">假设有两个 XXX<sub>1</sub> 和 XXX<sub>2</sub> 满足条件</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">然后再证 XXX<sub>1</sub> 和 XXX<sub>2</sub> 相等</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">唯一性的意义在于，只要满足这个形式，那么满足这个形式的值就一定是具有这个意义的值</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">好吧，这只是通俗的说法，可能会更好懂？</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">比如说如果凑成了满足泰勒的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x-x_0)^n$</math-renderer> 形式的系数项，那么这个系数项一定就是泰勒展开的唯一的系数项</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">比如如果凑成了满足 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$AB = E$</math-renderer> 形式的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$B$</math-renderer>，那么这个 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$B$</math-renderer> 一定是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$A$</math-renderer> 的唯一的逆矩阵</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-二常用不等式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#二常用不等式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-21-绝对值不等式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#21-绝对值不等式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.1 绝对值不等式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a, b$</math-renderer> 为实数，则：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\vert a\\pm b\\vert\\leqslant\\vert a\\vert+\\vert b\\vert$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">推广公式一到离散区间：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\vert a_1\\pm a_2\\pm a_3\\pm\\cdots\\pm a_n\\vert\\leqslant\\vert a_1\\vert+\\vert a_2\\vert+\\cdots+\\vert a_n\\vert$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">推广公式一到连续区间且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 $<a href=\"a%3Cb\">a,b</a>$ 上可积：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\vert\\int_a^bf(x)\\textrm{d}x\\vert\\leqslant\\int_a^b\\vert f(x)\\vert\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因为符号不一定相同的面积代数和一定小于同为正的面积代数和</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\vert\\vert a\\vert-\\vert b\\vert\\vert\\leqslant\\vert a-b\\vert$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">后式子为两点之差，前式子可以看作 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a$</math-renderer>、$b$ 两点与0之间的距离的差，若异号则两者必然抵消一部分，若同号则就等于后式</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-22-根号不等式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#22-根号不等式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.2 根号不等式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a,b,c&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer>：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sqrt{ab}\\leqslant\\dfrac{a+b}{2}\\leqslant\\sqrt{\\dfrac{a^2+b^2}{2}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">公式一非常重要，即算数平均值大几何平均值</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sqrt[3]{abc}\\leqslant\\dfrac{a+b+c}{3}\\leqslant\\dfrac{a^2+b^2+c^2}{3}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}\\sqrt[n]{a_1^n+a_2^n+...+a_m^n} = \\max_{1\\leqslant i \\leqslant m}{a_i} &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-23-指数不等式\" f</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.复合运算</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">代入法</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>3.初等函数</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由常数和基本初等函数经过有限次的四则运算或者有限次的符合运算构成的，且能用一个式子表达的函数，称为初等函数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.1.2 函数的性质</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">奇偶性</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = f(x)$</math-renderer> 关于直线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 对称 &lt;=&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a+x) = f(a-x)$</math-renderer> &lt;=&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a+x),f(a-x)$</math-renderer> 关于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 是偶函数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = f(x)$</math-renderer> 关于点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,0)$</math-renderer> 对称 &lt;=&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a+x) = -f(a-x)$</math-renderer> &lt;=&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a+x),f(a-x)$</math-renderer> 关于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 是偶函数</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有界性</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">常见有界函数：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert \\sin{x} \\rvert \\leqslant 1$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert \\cos{x} \\rvert \\leqslant 1$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert \\arcsin{x} \\rvert \\leqslant \\dfrac{\\pi}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0 \\leqslant \\arccos{x} \\leqslant \\pi$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$-\\dfrac{\\pi}{2} &amp;lt; \\arctan{x} &amp;lt; \\dfrac{\\pi}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0 &amp;lt; arccot{x} &amp;lt; \\pi$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">周期性</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">周期函数不一定存在最小正周期</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：狄利克雷函数</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">单调性</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-12-函数的性质的综合问题\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#12-函数的性质的综合问题\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.2 函数的性质的综合问题</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-121-函数运算对奇偶性的影响\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#121-函数运算对奇偶性的影响\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.2.1 函数运算对奇偶性的影响</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">奇函数的定义域关于原点对称，若包括原点，则必有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0) = -f(-0)$</math-renderer> 得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">故当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 为奇函数时，$f(x)$ 的原函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) + C$</math-renderer> 一定是偶函数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">而当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 为偶函数时，$f(x)$ 的原函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) + C$</math-renderer> 不一定是奇函数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">特殊函数：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) + f(-x)$</math-renderer> 是偶函数，$f(x) - f(-x)$ 是奇函数</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g_1(x) = \\dfrac{f(x)+f(-x)}{2},g_2(x) = \\dfrac{f(x)-f(-x)}{2},x \\in (-a,a)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = g_1(x) + g_2(x),x \\in (-a,a)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 可表示为一个偶函数与一个奇函数之和</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-122-判断函数有界性的方法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#122-判断函数有界性的方法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.2.2 判断函数有界性的方法</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上连续 =&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上有界</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内连续，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to a^+}f(x),\\lim_{x \\to b^-}f(x)$</math-renderer> 均存在 =&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内有界</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证：由 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to a^+}f(x),\\lim_{x \\to b^-}f(x)$</math-renderer> 均存在，根据极限的局部有界性，$f(x)$ 在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,a+\\delta_1),(b-\\delta_2,b),\\delta_1 &amp;gt; 0,\\delta_2 &amp;gt; 0,b-\\delta_2 &amp;gt; a+\\delta_1$</math-renderer> 内均有界</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又由 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内连续推出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a+\\delta_1,b-\\delta_2]$</math-renderer> 上连续</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">从而 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 有界</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 在有限区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内有界 =&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内有界，反之不一定成立</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例如：$f(x) = \\sqrt{x}$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(0,1)$</math-renderer> 内有界，但 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x) = \\dfrac{1}{2\\sqrt{x}}$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(0,1)$</math-renderer> 内无界</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证：$\\forall x \\in (a,b)$，取 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0 \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer>，由拉格朗日中值定理，可知</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = f(x_0) + f'(\\xi)(x - x_0),a &amp;lt; \\xi &amp;lt; b$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">故 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert f(x) \\rvert \\leqslant \\lvert f(x_0) \\rvert + \\lvert f'(\\xi) \\rvert \\lvert x - x_0 \\rvert$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 有界</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但若将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 改为无限区间，则结论不一定成立</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">辨析：无穷大必是无界量，但无界量不一定是无穷大</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{1}{x}\\sin{\\dfrac{1}{x}}$</math-renderer> 是无界量而不是无穷大</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-123-判断函数周期性的方法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#123-判断函数周期性的方法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.2.3 判断函数周期性的方法</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用周期性的定义</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 是可导的周期函数，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 有相同的周期</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 是以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$T$</math-renderer> 为周期的连续函数，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) = \\int_a^x{f(t)dt}$</math-renderer> 不一定是周期函数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例如：$f(x) = \\cos{x} + 1$ 是以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$2\\pi$</math-renderer> 为周期的周期函数，但 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^x(\\cos{t}+1)dt = \\sin{x} + x$</math-renderer> 不是周期函数</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-124-判别函数单调性的方法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#124-判别函数单调性的方法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.2.4 判别函数单调性的方法</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x) \\geqslant 0(\\leqslant 0)$</math-renderer>，且等号仅在有限多个点处成立，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在区间上单调增加（减少）</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-13-反函数\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#13-反函数\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.3 反函数</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y \\equiv f(f^{-1}(y)), x \\equiv f(f^{-1}(x))$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因为式中的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f^{-1}$</math-renderer> 之间不能夹系数，所以要凑</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">相关题目的核心思想就是凑成这个原函数嵌套反函数的性质</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x \\geqslant 0$</math-renderer> 时，函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 可导，有非负的反函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)$</math-renderer>，且恒等式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_1^{f(x)}{g(t)dt} = x^2 - 1$</math-renderer> 成立，求函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_1^{f(x)}{g(t)dt} = x^2 - 1$</math-renderer> 两边求导，得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(f(x))f'(x) = 2x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又由反函数的性质，$g(f(x)) = x$，得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$xf'(x) = 2x$</math-renderer> =&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = 2x+C$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">观察恒等式，取 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 1$</math-renderer> 时可以令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x^2 - 1 = 0$</math-renderer>，此时 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(1) = 2+C$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_1^{2+C}{g(t)dt} = 0$</math-renderer>，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$2+C = 1$</math-renderer> =&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$C = -1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = 2x-1$</math-renderer></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">还利用了 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^a{f(x)dx} = 0$</math-renderer> 的性质</p>\n</blockquote>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-14-函数极限的概念\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#14-函数极限的概念\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.4 函数极限的概念</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：定义 无穷大与无穷小 函数极限的性质与定理 计算方法</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-141-函数极限的定义\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#141-函数极限的定义\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.4.1 函数极限的定义</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">极限的定义是用“距离”刻画的</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">定义中的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varepsilon$</math-renderer> 具有任意性，$\\delta$ 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$X$</math-renderer> 具有存在性，$\\delta$ 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$X$</math-renderer> 一般与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varepsilon$</math-renderer> 有关</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用极限定义验证极限的存在性，关键是证明 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\delta$</math-renderer> 或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$X$</math-renderer> 的存在性</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0}f(x)$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 处是否有定义无关</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{x} = 1$</math-renderer>，则（）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">A. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">B. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(0) = 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">C. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}f(x) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">D. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}f'(x) = 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：C</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">极限式能够存在，说明 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 的去心邻域内是存在的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">也说明了 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}f(x) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是不知道 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 是否有定义，即使有定义，也不知道 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 是否连续</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">只有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 连续才能由 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}f(x) = 0$</math-renderer> 得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0) = 0$</math-renderer>，A 错</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">要求某点的导数，使用导数定义式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(0) = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x) - f(0)}{x - 0}$</math-renderer> 由于不知道 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0)$</math-renderer> 所以不知道导数定义式是否存在，B 错</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">只有知道 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(0) = 1$</math-renderer> 时再进一步知道 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 连续才能推出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}f'(x) = 1$</math-renderer>，D 错</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-142-基础四则运算\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#142-基础四则运算\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.4.2 基础四则运算</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.极限四则运算的条件是充分非必要条件</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例如：$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{1}{x^2} = \\infty, \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{\\cos{x}}{x^2} = \\infty$ 极限均不存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但极限 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}(\\dfrac{1}{x^2}-\\dfrac{\\cos{x}}{x^2}) = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{1-\\cos{x}}{x^2} = \\dfrac{1}{2}$</math-renderer> 存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.使用情景</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">极限非 0 的因子的极限可以先求</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim \\dfrac{g(x)}{f(x)} = \\dfrac{1}{A}\\lim{g(x)}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但对于</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim \\dfrac{f_1(x)+f_2(x)}{f_3(x)+f_4(x)}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f_i(x)$</math-renderer> 不能单独求</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$\\dfrac{e^{\\dfrac{2}{x}ln(1+x)}-e^2[1-ln(1+x)]}{x}, x \\rightarrow 0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中如果先令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$e^{\\dfrac{2}{x}ln(1+x)} \\rightarrow e^2$</math-renderer> 就会出错</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{e^{-x}(1+\\dfrac{1}{x})^{x^2}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">错误点 1：<strong>幂的嵌套运算理解错误</strong>，认为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{(1+\\dfrac{1}{x})^{x^2}} = \\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{[(1+\\dfrac{1}{x})^{x}]^2} = e^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">实际上 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a^{x^2} = a^{x·x} = (a^x)^x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{(1+\\dfrac{1}{x})^{x^2}} = \\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{[(1+\\dfrac{1}{x})^{x}]^x}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">错误点 2：<strong>忽略了双侧极限</strong>，认为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{e^{-x}} = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">很容易踩的坑！实际上 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}$</math-renderer> 包含 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to +\\infty}$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to -\\infty}$</math-renderer>，而 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to -\\infty}{e^{-x}} = \\infty, \\lim_{x \\to +\\infty}{e^{-x}} = 0$</math-renderer>，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{e^{-x}}$</math-renderer> 不存在（非无穷的不存在）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同理 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{(1+\\dfrac{1}{x})^{x^2}}$</math-renderer> 也不存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以不能使用极限的四则运算</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{e^{-x}(1+\\dfrac{1}{x})^{x^2}} = \\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{[e^{-1}(1+\\dfrac{1}{x})^x]^x} \\\n= \\exp{[x(\\ln(e^{-1}(1+\\dfrac{1}{x}))]} \\\n= \\exp{[x(\\ln{(1+\\dfrac{1}{x})}-1)]}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ln(1+x)$</math-renderer> 泰勒展开到两阶之后代入算得答案为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$e^{-1/2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于复杂的式子只能用泰勒展开了</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">具体展开的阶数都是试探出来的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">只要保证多余的项是趋向 0 不受干扰就行了</p>\n</blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>3.复合运算法则</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">函数的复合运算与极限运算交换顺序</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-143-函数极限的性质\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#143-函数极限的性质\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.4.3 函数极限的性质</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">唯一性</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有界性</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">保号性</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">保序性</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-144-无穷大与无穷小\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#144-无穷大与无穷小\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.4.4 无穷大与无穷小</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.无穷小</strong></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有界函数与无穷小之积是无穷小</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有限个无穷小之和是无穷小</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有限个无穷小之积是无穷小</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.函数极限与无穷小的关系</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim{f(x)} = A$</math-renderer> &lt;=&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = A + \\alpha$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>3.无穷小的比较</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>4.常用的等价无穷小</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>5.无穷大</strong></p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-15-函数极限的计算\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#15-函数极限的计算\"><svg class=\"octicon 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5 函数极限的计算</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-151-夹逼准则\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#151-夹逼准则\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5.1 夹逼准则</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">夹逼准则可以用来证明不等式也可以用来计算极限</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-152-重要极限\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#152-重要极限\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5.2 重要极限</h4>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-153-导数定义\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#153-导数定义\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5.3 导数定义</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">极限转换以及连续性的时候会用到，但是使用的频率也较小</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-154-等价无穷小替换\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#154-等价无穷小替换\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5.4 等价无穷小替换</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">与基础四则运算类似替换的必然是整个求极限的乘或除的因子，一般加减法与部分的因子不能进行等价无穷小替换</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果是判断等价无穷小的阶数则可以，因为只会相差一个更高阶的无穷小，不影响整体</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于无法直接得出变换式子的，可以对对应参数进行凑，以达到目标的可替换的等价无穷小</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">特殊情形：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例如：$y = \\sin{u},u = x\\sin{\\dfrac{1}{x}}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x \\to 0$</math-renderer> 时，$\\lim_{x \\to 0}{x\\sin{\\dfrac{1}{x}}} = 0,\\lim_{u \\to 0}{\\sin{u}} = 0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin{u}$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$u = x\\sin{\\dfrac{1}{x}}$</math-renderer> 均是无穷小，但 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin{(x\\sin{\\dfrac{1}{x}})}$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x\\sin{\\dfrac{1}{x}}$</math-renderer> 不是等价无穷小</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\sin{(x\\sin{\\dfrac{1}{x}})}}{x\\sin{\\dfrac{1}{x}}}$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 的去心邻域内有无穷多个点没有定义，如取 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = \\dfrac{1}{n\\pi}$</math-renderer>（$n$ 充分大），故不能求其极限</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-155-有理化\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#155-有理化\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5.5 有理化</h4>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-156-利用左右极限求极限\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#156-利用左右极限求极限\"><svg class=\"octicon 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5.6 利用左右极限求极限</h4>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-157-拉格朗日中值定理\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#157-拉格朗日中值定理\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5.7 拉格朗日中值定理</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">出现 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(b)-f(a)$</math-renderer> 的形式时可以考虑使用中值定理</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-158-洛必达法则\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#158-洛必达法则\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5.8 洛必达法则</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">洛必达法则的本质是降低商形式的极限式子的幂次。对于幂次高的式子必然使用洛必达法则</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">式子比较复杂最好不要使用洛必达法则，最好是对求导后有规律或幂次较低的式子进行上下求导</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于数列极限，应将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n$</math-renderer> （正整数）改为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> （实数），因为数列是离散的，所以不能对其求导数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">只有未定式才能使用洛必达，若已经能计算出为常数则不能使用洛必达</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果分子分母极限不存在且不是无穷，则洛必达法则失效，可能存在极限，换其他方法求解</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">洛必达法则必须使用在分子分母都趋向 0 或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\infty$</math-renderer> 时，如果不是这样的趋向则不能使用</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-159-泰勒公式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#159-泰勒公式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.5.9 泰勒公式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">泰勒公式一般会使用趋向 0 的麦克劳林公式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">泰勒展开嵌套时要保证截取的多项式的系数唯一</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$\\dfrac{e^{\\dfrac{2}{x}ln(1+x)}-e^2[1-ln(1+x)]}{x}, x \\rightarrow 0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">展开：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{2}{x}ln(1+x) = \\dfrac{2}{x}(0+x-\\dfrac{1}{2}x^2+\\dfrac{1}{3}x^3+o(x^3)) = 2-x+\\dfrac{2}{3}x^2+o(x^2)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Rightarrow \\dfrac{2}{x}ln(1+x) -2 = -x+\\dfrac{2}{3}x^2+o(x^2)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">嵌套进</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$e^x = 1+x+\\dfrac{1}{2}x^2+\\dfrac{1}{6}x^3+o(x^3)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Rightarrow e^x - 1 = x+\\dfrac{1}{2}x^2+\\dfrac{1}{6}x^3+o(x^3)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$e^{\\dfrac{2}{x}ln(1+x) -2} - 1 = [-x+\\dfrac{2}{3}x^2+o(x^2)] + \\dfrac{1}{2}[-x+\\dfrac{2}{3}x^2+o(x^2)]^2 + \\dfrac{1}{6}[-x+\\dfrac{2}{3}x^2+o(x^2)]^3+o(x^3)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这个时候不需要把这个嵌套式子展开，而是只需要看幂为 k 的项的各个来源相加</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例如要看幂为 2，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[-x+\\dfrac{2}{3}x^2+o(x^2)]$</math-renderer> 中有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{2}{3}x^2$</math-renderer>，但是在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{2}[-x+\\dfrac{2}{3}x^2+o(x^2)]^2$</math-renderer> 中还有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{2}x^2$</math-renderer>，而在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{6}[-x+\\dfrac{2}{3}x^2+o(x^2)]^3$</math-renderer> 中肯定没有幂为 2 的项，之后就不用看了</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-16-函数极限的化简\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#16-函数极限的化简\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.6 函数极限的化简</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-161-对数法则\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#161-对数法则\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.6.1 对数法则</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\log_n(a\\cdot b)=\\log_n a+\\log_n 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.6.2 指数法则</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当出现 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)^{g(x)}$</math-renderer> 的类似幂函数与指数函数类型的式子，需要使用 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$u^v=e^{v\\ln u}$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\"
