.751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.6.6 有理化</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">和差形式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sqrt{a}\\pm\\sqrt{b}=\\dfrac{a+b}{\\sqrt{a}\\mp\\sqrt{b}}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">乘积形式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">此时带有根号的式子只有单个没有加上或减去另一个式子，所以就需要将其转换为和差形式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求极限 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{n\\to\\infty}\\sin^2(\\pi\\sqrt{n^2+n})$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">根据三角函数中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x\\pm n\\pi$</math-renderer> 结果不变，原式变为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$=\\lim\\limits_{n\\to\\infty}\\sin^2[\\pi(\\sqrt{n^2+n}-n)]$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-167-换元法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#167-换元法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.6.7 换元法</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">换元法本身没什么技巧性，主要是更方便计算。最重要的是获取到共有的最大因子进行替换</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求极限 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{x\\to 1^-}\\ln x\\ln(1-x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x\\to 0$</math-renderer>，$\\ln(1+x)\\sim x$，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x\\to 1$</math-renderer>，$\\ln x\\sim x-1$</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-168-倒代换\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#168-倒代换\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.6.8 倒代换</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">含有分式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当极限式子中含有分式中一般都需要用其倒数，把分式换成整式方便计算</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\infty-\\infty$</math-renderer> 型</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\infty\\cdot\\infty$</math-renderer> 型</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-169-拆项\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#169-拆项\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.6.9 拆项</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">拆项需要根据式子形式进行，所以很难找到普遍规律</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">积拆项</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">和拆项</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求$\\lim\\limits_{x\\to 0}\\dfrac{1-\\cos x\\sqrt{\\cos 2x}\\sqrt[3]{\\cos 3x}}{\\ln\\cos x}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：使用 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\cos x-1\\sim\\dfrac{x^2}{2}, 1-\\sqrt{x} \\sim 1-\\dfrac{1}{2}x^2, 1-\\sqrt[3]{x} \\sim 1-\\dfrac{1}{3}x^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{x\\to 0}\\dfrac{1-\\cos x\\sqrt{\\cos 2x}\\sqrt[3]{\\cos 3x}}{\\ln\\cos x}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$=\\lim\\limits_{x\\to 0}\\dfrac{1-\\cos x+\\cos x-\\cos x\\sqrt{\\cos 2x}\\sqrt[3]{\\cos 3x}}{-\\dfrac{x^2}{2}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$=\\lim\\limits_{x\\to 0}\\dfrac{\\dfrac{x^2}{2}}{-\\dfrac{x^2}{2}}+\\dfrac{\\cos x(1-\\sqrt{\\cos 2x}\\sqrt[3]{\\cos 3x})}{-\\dfrac{x^2}{2}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$=-1+\\lim\\limits_{x\\to 0}\\dfrac{(1-\\sqrt{\\cos 2x})+\\sqrt{\\cos 2x}-\\sqrt{\\cos 2x}\\sqrt[3]{\\cos 3x}}{-\\dfrac{x^2}{2}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$=-1+\\lim\\limits_{x\\to 0}\\dfrac{-\\dfrac{1}{2}(\\cos 2x-1)+\\sqrt{\\cos 2x}(1-\\sqrt[3]{\\cos 3x})}{-\\dfrac{x^2}{2}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$=-1+\\lim\\limits_{x\\to 0}\\dfrac{-\\dfrac{1}{2}(-\\dfrac{4x^2}{2})+\\left(-\\dfrac{1}{3}\\right)\\left(-\\dfrac{9x^2}{2}\\right)}{-\\dfrac{x^2}{2}}=-6$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-1610-脱帽法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#1610-脱帽法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.6.10 脱帽法</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">函数中有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer>，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 无法转换出常数项。则将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 利用已知的极限值转换为一个函数加上高阶无穷小的形式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$\\lim\\limits_{x\\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{x} = 3$，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = 3x + o(x^2)$</math-renderer></p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-17-极限路径的理解\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#17-极限路径的理解\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.7 极限路径的理解</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$\nf(x) = \\left{\n\\begin{array}{lcl}\nx^2\\sin(1/x), &amp; x \\ne 0 \\\n0, &amp; x = 0\n\\end{array}\n\\right.\n$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">应用拉格朗日中值定理得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) - f(0) = f'(\\xi)(x-0), 0&amp;lt;\\xi&amp;lt;x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x^2\\sin(1/x) = [2\\xi\\sin(1/\\xi) - \\cos(1/\\xi)]x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x\\sin(1/x) = 2\\xi\\sin(1/\\xi) - \\cos(1/\\xi)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x \\to 0^+$</math-renderer> 时，$\\xi \\to 0^+$，由上式得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{\\xi \\to 0^+}\\xi\\sin(1/\\xi) = 0 = \\lim_{\\xi \\to 0^+}[2\\xi\\sin(1/\\xi) - \\cos(1/\\xi)]$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{\\xi \\to 0^+}\\cos(1/\\xi) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">是否可以得出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0^+}\\cos(1/x) = 0$</math-renderer>？</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">不可，$\\xi$ 是一个特殊函数，只代表一种趋向 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0^+$</math-renderer> 的路径，不代表任意路径</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-18-数列极限的计算\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#18-数列极限的计算\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.8 数列极限的计算</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：定义 极限的性质 证明极限存在的方法 计算方法</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-181-用单调有界准则求极限\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#181-用单调有界准则求极限\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.8.1 用单调有界准则求极限</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">1.简单通项公式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.复杂递推公式</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">许多题目只给出样子，连通项公式都不会给出，只会给出一个复杂递推公式，其中包括开根号，倒数，甚至只是举例。这种题目就必须使用单调有界准则来完成，甚至还需要其他的技巧</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">难点就是确认上下界</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">判断单调性时，根式用乘除，和式用加减</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">确认上下界和单调性后，设极限为 k，令递推公式中的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_{n+1}, x_{n}$</math-renderer> = k，解得 k</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">可以先求极限 k，然后射箭画靶，在上一步的上下界证明中照着 k 来思考</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求出数列 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sqrt{2}$</math-renderer>，$\\sqrt{2+\\sqrt{2}}$，$\\sqrt{2+\\sqrt{2+\\sqrt{2}}}\\cdots$ 的极限</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">根据数列样式，无法通过普通的通项公式来表达，所以需要考虑使用递推式来表示：$x_{n+1}=\\sqrt{2+x_n}$。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">首先证明有界性：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">给定一个任意的正整数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$k$</math-renderer>，再根据递推式，假定 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_k&amp;lt;2$</math-renderer>，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_{k+1}=\\sqrt{2+x_k}&amp;lt;\\sqrt{2+2}=2$</math-renderer>。且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_1=\\sqrt{2}$</math-renderer> 满足假定，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_k&amp;lt;2$</math-renderer> 对于任意的正整数$k$都成立，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_n$</math-renderer> 存在上界 2。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">然后证明单调性，根据其递推式：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_{n+1}-x_n=\\sqrt{2+x_n}-x_n=\\dfrac{2+x_n-x_n^2}{\\sqrt{2+x_n}+x_n}=\\dfrac{-(x_n-2)(x_n+1)}{\\sqrt{2+x_n}+x_n}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0&amp;lt;x_n&amp;lt;2$</math-renderer>，从而上式子大于 0，从而数列单调递增</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以根据单调有界定理，数列 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_{n+1}=\\sqrt{2+x_n}$</math-renderer> 一定存在极限，令其极限值 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{n\\to\\infty}x_n=a$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">将递推式两边平方并取极限：$\\lim\\limits_{n\\to\\infty}x^2_{n+1}=\\lim\\limits_{n\\to\\infty}(2+x_n)$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">从而 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a^2=2+a$</math-renderer>，得出 a = 2 （根据极限的保号性 -1 被舍去）</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求单调性也不一定要用定义</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求有界可以利用单调性</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_1=\\sqrt{a}$</math-renderer>（$a&gt;0$），$x_{n+1}=\\sqrt{a+x_n}$，求极限</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_1=\\sqrt{a}$</math-renderer>，$x_2=\\sqrt{a+\\sqrt{a}}$，$a_n=\\sqrt{a+\\cdots\\sqrt{a+\\sqrt{a}}}$ 所以可得单调递增（就这么直接说……）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_{n+1}=\\sqrt{a+x_n}$</math-renderer>，$x_{n+1}^2=a+x_n$，$x_{n+1}=\\dfrac{a}{x_{n+1}}+\\dfrac{x_n}{x_{n+1}}$。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由单调性 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_{n+1}\\geqslant x_n\\geqslant x_1=\\sqrt{a}$</math-renderer>，$x_{n+1}\\leqslant\\dfrac{a}{x_{n+1}}+1\\leqslant\\sqrt{a}+1$，即有上界。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">单调有界准则，$a_n$ 单调增且有上界，令极限为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$A$</math-renderer>，$A=\\sqrt{a+A}$，解得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$A=\\dfrac{1\\pm\\sqrt{1+4a}}{2}$</math-renderer>，负根舍去。</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$x_1=a\\geqslant0$，$y_1=b\\geqslant0$，$a\\leqslant b$，$x_{n+1}=\\sqrt{x_ny_n}$，$y_{n+1}=\\dfrac{x_n+y_n}{2}$（$n=1,2,\\cdots$），证明 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{n\\to\\infty}x_n=\\lim\\limits_{n\\to\\infty}y_n$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">算数平均值大几何平均值，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_{n+1} = \\sqrt{x_ny_n} &amp;lt; \\dfrac{x_n+y_n}{2} = y_{n+1}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_n &amp;lt; y_n$</math-renderer> 恒成立，则</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_{n+1} = \\sqrt{x_ny_n} &amp;gt; x_{n+1} = \\sqrt{x_n x_n} &amp;gt; x_n$</math-renderer>，即 x 单调递增</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y_{n+1}=\\dfrac{x_n+y_n}{2} &amp;lt; \\dfrac{y_n+y_n}{2} = y_n$</math-renderer>，即 y 单调递减</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_{n+1}^2=x_ny_n$</math-renderer>，$x_{n+1}=\\dfrac{x_n}{x_{n+1}}y_n\\leqslant y_n=b$，$\\therefore x_n$ 有上界。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y_{n+1}=\\dfrac{x_n+y_n}{2}$</math-renderer>，$x_n+y_n=2y_{n+1}$，$y_n=x_n-2y_{n+1}$，又 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y_n$</math-renderer> 单调递减，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y_{n+1}\\leqslant y_n$</math-renderer>，$\\therefore y_n\\geqslant x_n-2y_n$，$3y_n\\geqslant x_n$，$\\therefore y_n$ 有下界。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以根据单调有界准则，都有极限，令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{n\\to\\infty}x_n=A$</math-renderer>，$\\lim\\limits_{n\\to\\infty}y_n=B$。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">代入第二个式子，$B=\\dfrac{A+B}{2}$，解得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$A=B$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-182-用夹逼准则求极限\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#182-用夹逼准则求极限\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.8.2 用夹逼准则求极限</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.调整放缩程度</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}\\dfrac {1!+2!+...+(n-1)!}{n!}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">首先肯定知道 &gt; 0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">然后要放大，我只能想到</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac {1!+2!+...+(n-1)!}{n!} &amp;lt; \\dfrac {(n-1)(n-1)!}{n!} = \\dfrac{n-1}{n} = 1-\\dfrac{1}{n}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这样就放到 1 了……</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案是</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac {1!+2!+...+(n-1)!}{n!} = \\dfrac {1!+2!+...+(n-2)!+(n-1)!}{n!} &amp;lt; \\dfrac {(n-2)(n-2)! + (n-1)!}{n!} &amp;lt; \\dfrac{2(n-1)!}{n!} = \\dfrac{2}{n} \\rightarrow 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">可见有的时候稍微少放大一点会得到很好的效果</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-183-根据子列极限情况推导原数列极限情况\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#183-根据子列极限情况推导原数列极限情况\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.8.3 根据子列极限情况推导原数列极限情况</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">取两个不同子列，若子列极限不存在或存在但不相等，则原数列极限不存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若子列极限存在且相等，则原数列极限不一定存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">特例：两个子列分别取奇数项和偶数项，若子列极限存在且相等，则原数列极限存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因为奇数项和偶数项覆盖了所有路径</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-184-海涅定理归结原则\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#184-海涅定理归结原则\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.8.4 海涅定理（归结原则）</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">描述了函数极限与数列极限之间的关系</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0}f(x) = A$</math-renderer> &lt;=&gt;</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于同时满足以下三个条件的任意数列 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">${x_n}$</math-renderer>，都有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}f(x_n) = A$</math-renderer></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\forall n \\in N^+, x_n \\ne x_0$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\forall n \\in N^+, f(x_n)$</math-renderer> 有定义</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}x_n = x_0$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">也就是</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">x 连续地趋向一点时，函数存在 &lt;=&gt;</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">x 沿任意路径离散地趋向一点时，函数存在</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-185-使用四则运算化简极限式中的部分项\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#185-使用四则运算化简极限式中的部分项\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.8.5 使用四则运算化简极限式中的部分项</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{\\sqrt{n}{a^n+b^n+...+c^n}} = \\max{a,b,...,c}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$X = \\sqrt{n}{a^n+b^n+...+c^n}$</math-renderer> 两边乘 n 次幂，有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$X^n = a^n+b^n+...+c^n$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$M = \\max{a,b,...,c}$</math-renderer>，两边同除 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$M^n$</math-renderer>，有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(\\dfrac{X}{M})^n = (\\dfrac{a}{M})^n + (\\dfrac{b}{M})^n + ... + (\\dfrac{c}{M})^n$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">右式中一定包含一项 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(\\dfrac{\\max{a,b,...,c}}{M})^n = 1^n = 1$</math-renderer>，其他项 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\to 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因此左式也 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\to 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因此 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$X \\to M = \\max{a,b,...,c}$</math-renderer></p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-19-n-项和\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#19-n-项和\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.9 n 项和</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-191-倒序相加法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#191-倒序相加法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.9.1 倒序相加法</h4>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-192-公式法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" dir=\"auto\">将数列的一项拆成两项或多项，使得前后项相抵消，留下有限项</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-194-错位相减法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#194-错位相减法\"><svg class=\"octicon 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.9.4 错位相减法</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">应用于等比数列与等差数列相乘的形式</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-195-迭加法\" class=\"anchor\" .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.9.5 迭加法</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a_{n+1} = a_n +f(n)$</math-renderer> 转化为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a_{n+1}-a_n = f(n)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">迭加：$a_{n+1} - a_1 = \\sum_{i = 1}^n{f(i)}$</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-196-分组求和法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#196-分组求和法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.9.6 分组求和法</h4>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-197-构造法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#197-构造法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.9.7 构造法</h4>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-198-利用定积分的定义求极限\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#198-利用定积分的定义求极限\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.9.8 利用定积分的定义求极限</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">上面那些方法都是高中学过的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这个才是高数里出现的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int^1_0{f(x)}dx=\\lim_{\\lambda \\to 0}\\sum_{k=1}^n{f(\\xi_k)\\Delta x_k = \\lim_{n \\rightarrow \\infty}\\sum_{k=1}^n{f(\\dfrac{k}{n})\\dfrac{1}{n}} = \\lim_{n \\rightarrow \\infty}\\dfrac{1}{n}}\\sum_{k=1}^n{f(\\dfrac{k}{n})}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">直接找公共的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{n}$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{k}{n}$</math-renderer> 看上去挺简单</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是有的时候还需要一点反向思维，例如，把一个积分拆成求和式，来方便化简等</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$A_n = \\dfrac{n}{n^2+1} + \\dfrac{n}{n^2+2^2} + ... + \\dfrac{n}{n^2+n^2}$</math-renderer>，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}{n(\\dfrac{\\pi}{4}-A_n)}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = \\dfrac{1}{1+x^2}$</math-renderer>，因为</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$A_n = \\dfrac{1}{n}\\sum_{i=1}^n{\\dfrac{1}{1+\\dfrac{i^2}{n^2}}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">故 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}A_n = \\int_0^1f(x)dx = \\dfrac{\\pi}{4}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">记 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_i=\\dfrac{i}{n}$</math-renderer>，则</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$A_n = \\sum_{i=1}^n\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}f(x_i)dx$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$J_n = n(\\dfrac{\\pi}{4}-A_n)$</math-renderer>，故</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$J_n = n\\sum_{i=1}^n\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}(f(x)-f(x_i))dx$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由拉格朗日中值定理，存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_i \\in (x_{i-1},x_i)$</math-renderer> 使得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$J_n = n\\sum_{i=1}^n\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}f'(\\xi_i)(x-x_i)dx$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$m_i$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$M_i$</math-renderer> 分别是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[x_{i-1},x_i]$</math-renderer> 上的最小值和最大值，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$m_i \\leqslant f'(\\xi_i) \\leqslant M_i$</math-renderer>，故积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}f'(\\xi_i)(x-x_i)dx$</math-renderer> 介于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}m_i(x-x_i)dx$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}M_i(x-x_i)dx$</math-renderer> 之间，所以存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\eta_i \\in (x_{i-1},x_i)$</math-renderer> 使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}f'(\\xi_i)(x-x_i)dx = \\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}f'(\\eta_i)(x-x_i)dx$</math-renderer>，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(\\xi_i)$</math-renderer> 对于 dx 的积分来说是一个变量，而 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(\\eta_i)$</math-renderer> 对于 dx 的积分来说是一个常量</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}f'(\\eta_i)(x-x_i)dx = f'(\\eta_i)\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}(x-x_i)dx = f'(\\eta_i)(\\dfrac{1}{2}x^2 - x_i)\\vert_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i} = \\dfrac{-f'(\\eta_i)(x_i-x_{i-1})^2}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{x_{i-1}}^{x_i}f'(\\xi_i)(x-x_i)dx = \\dfrac{-f'(\\eta_i)(x_i-x_{i-1})^2}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">于是，$J_n = -\\dfrac{n}{2}\\sum_{i=1}^nf'(\\eta_i)(x_i-x_{i-1})^2 = -\\dfrac{1}{2n}\\sum_{i=1}^nf'(\\eta_i)$，从而</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}{n(\\dfrac{\\pi}{4}-A_n)} = \\lim_{n \\to \\infty}J_n = -\\dfrac{1}{2}\\int_0^1f'(x)dx = -\\dfrac{1}{2}[f(1)-f(0)] = \\dfrac{1}{4}$</math-renderer></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">甚至是有点时候我会以为我算不出来是因为我没有找到一个合适的放缩方法，而根本没有想到要用定积分的定义</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">只能说，看到 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{n}$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{n},\\dfrac{2}{n},...,\\dfrac{n}{n}$</math-renderer> 这种标志就要提高警惕……</p>\n</blockquote>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-110-n-项连乘\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#110-n-项连乘\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.10 n 项连乘</h3>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">消去分子分母中的公因子</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">取对数化为 n 项和</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">逐步消去</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a_n = \\cos{\\dfrac{\\theta}{2}} · \\cos{\\dfrac{\\theta}{2^2}} · ... · \\cos{\\dfrac{\\theta}{2^n}}$</math-renderer>，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}a_n$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">本来我是瞬间想到那个 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin{x}\\sin{2x}\\sin{4x}$</math-renderer>，然后我都知道我要用二倍角逐步消去了</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是我顺着这个思路想到的是，一开始要乘 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin{\\dfrac{\\theta}{2}}$</math-renderer> 之后显然我就没办法做下去了……</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">实际上一开始乘 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin{\\dfrac{\\theta}{2^n}}$</math-renderer> 就好了</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-111-连续\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#111-连续\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.11 连续</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：定义 连续相关定理 间断点的分类</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.定义</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0}f(x) = f(x_0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">则称 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = x_0$</math-renderer> 连续</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.性质</strong></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有界性定理</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">最值定理</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">介值定理</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">零点定理</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-112-间断点\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#112-间断点\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.12 间断点</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = x_0$</math-renderer> 处不存在，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = x_0$</math-renderer> 是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 的一个间断点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第一类间断点 左右极限都存在</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">可去间断点 左右极限相等</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">跳跃间断点 左右极限不相等</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第二类间断点 左右极限至少有一个不存在</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-113-由极限定义的函数\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#113-由极限定义的函数\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.13 由极限定义的函数</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-1131-先求极限再研究具体表达式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#1131-先求极限再研究具体表达式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.13.1 先求极限再研究具体表达式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = \\lim_{n \\to \\infty}{\\dfrac{1-x^{2n}}{1+x^{2n}}x}$</math-renderer>（n 为正整数），则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 有（）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">A. 两个第二类间断点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">B. 一个第一类间断点，一个第二类间断点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">C. 两个第一类间断点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">D. 零个间断点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：C</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert x \\rvert &amp;lt; 1$</math-renderer> 时，$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}x^{2n} \\to 0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert x \\rvert = 1$</math-renderer> 时，$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}x^{2n} = 1$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert x \\rvert &amp;gt; 1$</math-renderer> 时，$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}x^{2n} \\to +\\infty$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">则有 $f(x) = \\lim_{n \\to \\infty}{\\dfrac{1-x^{2n}}{1+x^{2n}}x} = \\left{\n\\begin{array}{lcl}\n-x, \\lvert x \\rvert &gt; 1 \\\n0, \\lvert x \\rvert = 1 \\\nx, \\lvert x \\rvert &lt; 1\n\\end{array}\n\\right.$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">易错点：认为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{1+x^{2n}}$</math-renderer> 对任意 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 有意义，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 不可能存在间断点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">实际上，因为这是包含极限的函数，所以<strong>必须先把极限求出来，然后再研究具体表达式</strong></p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">极限内的部分是否有定义同样也会影响这个由极限定义的函数是否有定义，例如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = \\lim_{t \\to 0}(1+\\dfrac{\\sin{t}}{x})^{\\dfrac{x^2}{t}} = e^x$</math-renderer>，但 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 处没有定义</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-1132-先由已知极限求-fx-的包含无穷小量的表达式再代入待求极限计算\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#1132-先由已知极限求-fx-的包含无穷小量的表达式再代入待求极限计算\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.13.2 先由已知极限求 f(x) 的包含无穷小量的表达式，再代入待求极限计算</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：已知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{\\sin{6x}-\\tan{x}·f(x)}{x^3} = 0$</math-renderer>，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{6 -f(x)}{x^2}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：38</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">已知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\sin{6x}-\\tan{x}·f(x)}{x^3} = 0 + \\alpha(x)$</math-renderer>，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\alpha(x) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">故 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = \\dfrac{\\sin{6x} - x^3\\alpha(x)}{\\tan{x}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">代入待求极限：$\\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{6 -f(x)}{x^2}} = \\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{6 -\\dfrac{\\sin{6x} - x^3\\alpha(x)}{\\tan{x}}}{x^2}} = \\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{6\\tan{x} -\\sin{6x}}{x^3}} = ...$</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-1133-根据趋向某点的极限得到在该点的函数值导数值\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#1133-根据趋向某点的极限得到在该点的函数值导数值\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.13.3 根据趋向某点的极限得到在该点的函数值，导数值</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 是三次多项式，且有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 2a}{\\dfrac{f(x)}{x-2a}} = \\lim_{x \\to 4a}{\\dfrac{f(x)}{x - 4a}} = 1,a \\ne 0$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 3a}{\\dfrac{f(x)}{x - 3a}}$</math-renderer> =</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">容易知道，$f(x)$ 是连续的，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(2a) = \\lim_{x \\to 2a}f(x) = 0$</math-renderer>，同理有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(4a) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同时由这个极限式子还可以得到导数值，但是不是用洛比达哦，洛比达的因果关系是从未定型上下求导的结果之后反推回未定型的值的，不是先知道未定型的结果再得到未定型上下求导的结果的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以应该使用导数的定义：$f'(2a) = \\lim_{x \\to 2a}\\dfrac{f(x)-f(2a)}{x-2a} = \\lim_{x \\to 2a}{\\dfrac{f(x)}{x-2a}} = 1$，同理 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(4a) = 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 是三次多项式，已知两个零点，所以设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = k(x-2a)(x-4a)(x-\\alpha)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x) = k[(x-4a)(x-\\alpha) + (x-2a)(x-\\alpha) + (x-2a)(x-4a)]$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(2a) = f'(4a) = 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\alpha = 3a$</math-renderer>，于是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = k(x-2a)(x-3a)(x-4a)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又因为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 2a}{\\dfrac{f(x)}{x-2a}} = \\lim_{x \\to 2a}{\\dfrac{k(x-2a)(x-3a)(x-4a)}{x-2a}} = \\lim_{x \\to 2a}{k(x-3a)(x-4a)} = k2a^2 = 1$</math-renderer> =&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$k = \\dfrac{1}{2a^2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = \\dfrac{1}{2a^2}(x-2a)(x-3a)(x-4a)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因此 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 3a}{\\dfrac{f(x)}{x - 3a}} = \\lim_{x \\to 3a}{\\dfrac{\\dfrac{1}{2a^2}(x-2a)(x-3a)(x-4a)}{x - 3a}} = \\lim_{x \\to 3a}\\dfrac{1}{2a^2}(x-2a)(x-4a) = -\\dfrac{1}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-114-常用结论\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#114-常用结论\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.14 常用结论</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-1141-常用求和公式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#1141-常用求和公式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.14.1 常用求和公式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$1^2 + 2^2 + ... + n^2 = \\dfrac{1}{6}n(n+1)(2n+1)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$1^3 + 2^3 + ... + n^3 = [\\dfrac{n(n+1)}{2}]^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sum_{k=1}^n{k(k+1)} = \\dfrac{1}{3}n(n+1)(n+2)$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-1142-常用裂项公式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#1142-常用裂项公式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>1.14.2 常用裂项公式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{n(n+1)} = \\dfrac{1}{n}-\\dfrac{1}{n+1}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{n(n+1)(n+2)} = \\dfrac{1}{2}[\\dfrac{1}{n(n+1)}-\\dfrac{1}{(n+1)(n+2)}]$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{\\sqrt{n+1}+\\sqrt{n}} = \\sqrt{n+1}-\\sqrt{n}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{(a-1)a^n}{(a^n+b)(a^{n+1}+b)} = \\dfrac{1}{a^n+b} + \\dfrac{1}{a^{n+1}+b}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\log_a{\\dfrac{a_{n+1}}{a_n}} = \\log_a{a_{n+1}} - \\log_a{a_n}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(1+\\tan{a_{n+1}}\\tan{a_n})\\tan{(a_{n+1}-a_n)} = \\tan{a_{n+1}} - \\tan{a_n}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n·n! = (n+1)! - n!$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$C_n^{m-1} = C_{n+1}^m - C_n^m$</math-renderer></p>\n<h2 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-第二章-一元函数微分学\" class=\"anchor\" .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>第二章 一元函数微分学</h2>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a
