inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{g(x)}$</math-renderer> 不存在（不包括 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\infty$</math-renderer> 的不存在）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>5.$f(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 可导，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 邻域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$U(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内不一定可导</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 可导不是洛比达的条件，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 去心领域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\mathring{U}(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内可导才是</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以注意，如果题目给出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x_0), g'(x_0)$</math-renderer> 存在，但没有给出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x), g(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 去心领域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\mathring{U}(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内可导，那么不能使用洛比达，而应该使用凑成导数的形式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>6.不一定需要 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x), g'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 连续</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x), g'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 连续可以推出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x), g'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 邻域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$U(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内存在，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x), g(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 去心领域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\mathring{U}(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内可导，即满足洛比达条件</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x), g'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 不连续，也可能有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x), g'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 邻域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$U(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内存在，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x), g(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 去心领域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\mathring{U}(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内可导，即满足洛比达条件</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">也就是说 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x), g'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 连续只是一个更强的条件而已</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">也就是说，不能认为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x), g'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 不连续就不能用洛比达</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所谓：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">n 阶可导只能洛到 n - 1 阶</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">n 阶连续可以洛到 n 阶</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这个规律没错，但它很容易导致“$f'(x), g'(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 不连续就不能用洛比达”的错误认识</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">它的“n 阶可导只能洛到 n - 1 阶”的意思有两个</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提醒注意：<strong>已知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 可导，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 去心领域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\mathring{U}(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内不一定可导</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">而不是：$f'(x), g'(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 不连续就不能用洛比达</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">而“n 阶连续可以洛到 n 阶”是因为“$f'(x), g'(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 连续是一个更强的条件”，所以自然可以洛比达。这同样也不能说明“$f'(x), g'(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 不连续就不能用洛比达”</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提醒注意：已知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 可导，若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 去心领域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\mathring{U}(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内可导，那么确实可以使用洛比达 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{g(x)} = \\lim_{x \\to x_0}\\dfrac{f'(x)}{g'(x)}$</math-renderer>，<strong>但 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 不一定连续，因此不一定有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0}{f'(x)} = f'(x_0)$</math-renderer>，也就是极限是否存在还是未知的，洛成 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0}\\dfrac{f'(x)}{g'(x)}$</math-renderer> 不一定能用极限的四则运算计算 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\lim_{x \\to x_0}f'(x)}{\\lim_{x \\to x_0}g'(x)}$</math-renderer></strong></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有个文章举了一个例子：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x), g(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 邻域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$U(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内连续，$f(x), g(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 去心领域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\mathring{U}(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内可导，$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{x} = -1, \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{g(x)}{f^2(x)} = 1$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{x} = -1$</math-renderer> 可见 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}f(x)$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}x = o(x)$</math-renderer> 是同阶无穷小，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}f(x) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又因为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 连续，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由导数的定义式，$f'(0) = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x)-f(0)}{x-0} = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{x} = -1$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">洛比达，$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{x} = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f'(x)}{1} = -1$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">他说这样就推出来了 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}f(x) = -1 = f'(0)$</math-renderer> 所以推出来了 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 连续，比题目中给的“$f(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 去心领域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\mathring{U}(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内可导”条件更强了，所以他肯定哪里写错了</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">然后他就说只能是他洛比达写错了，恩，我认同</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">然后他说他洛比达哪里错了呢，他说是因为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 没有在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 连续导致的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但我觉得，这明显是因果关系上的错误吧，洛比达因果关系是由 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0}\\dfrac{f'(x)}{g'(x)} = A$</math-renderer>（或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\infty$</math-renderer>）推出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{g(x)} = A$</math-renderer>（或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\infty$</math-renderer>），而不是相反</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">现在他拿 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x)}{x} = -1$</math-renderer> 说洛比达之后的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{f'(x)}{x'} = -1$</math-renderer>，这不就是因果颠倒了吗，跟连续不连续没关系吧</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 处可导，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a) &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer>，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}[\\dfrac{f(a+\\dfrac{1}{x})}{f(a)}]^x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">错误解法：$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}[\\dfrac{f(a+\\dfrac{1}{x})}{f(a)}]^x = \\lim_{x \\to \\infty}\\exp{(x\\ln\\dfrac{f(a+\\dfrac{1}{x})}{f(a)})} = \\lim_{x \\to \\infty}\\exp{(\\dfrac{\\ln f(a+\\dfrac{1}{x}) - \\ln f(a)}{\\dfrac{1}{x}})} = \\lim_{t \\to 0}\\exp{(\\dfrac{\\ln f(a+t) - \\ln f(a)}{t})}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">错误点 1：根据导数定义：$\\lim_{t \\to 0}\\exp{(\\dfrac{\\ln f(a+t) - \\ln f(a)}{t})} = \\exp{[(\\ln{f(x)})']\\vert_{x = a}} = \\exp(\\dfrac{f'(a)}{f(a)})$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">错误在于只知道 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 处可导，而不知道 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ln f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 处是否可导</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">错误点 2：企图绕过导数定义，想要使用洛比达：$\\lim_{t \\to 0}\\exp{(\\dfrac{\\ln f(a+t) - \\ln f(a)}{t})} = \\lim_{t \\to 0}\\exp{(\\dfrac{[\\ln f(a+t)]'}{t'})} = \\lim_{t \\to 0}\\exp(\\dfrac{f'(a+t)}{f(a+t)}) = \\exp(\\dfrac{f'(a)}{f(a)})$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">错误在于：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第一，如果能够使用洛比达的话，那么本身就需要 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ln f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 处可导，那本身就可以直接使用导数定义式了；</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第二，就算已知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ln f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 处可导的同时又不用导数定义式，那么 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{t \\to 0}\\exp(\\dfrac{f'(a+t)}{f(a+t)}) = \\exp(\\dfrac{f'(a)}{f(a)})$</math-renderer> 这一步又进一步要求更强的条件：$f'(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 连续，这也是未知的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">正确解法：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">使用重要极限：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}[\\dfrac{f(a+\\dfrac{1}{x})}{f(a)}]^x = \\lim_{x \\to \\infty}[1 + \\dfrac{f(a+\\dfrac{1}{x})}{f(a)}- 1]^x \\\n= \\lim_{x \\to \\infty}[1 + (\\dfrac{f(a+\\dfrac{1}{x})}{f(a)}- 1)]^{1/(\\frac{f(a+\\frac{1}{x})}{f(a)}- 1)·(\\frac{f(a+\\frac{1}{x})}{f(a)}- 1)·x} \\\n= \\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{\\exp((\\dfrac{f(a+\\dfrac{1}{x})}{f(a)}- 1)x)} \\\n= \\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{\\exp(\\dfrac{1}{f(a)}\\dfrac{f(a+\\dfrac{1}{x})-f(a)}{\\dfrac{1}{x}})} \\\n= \\lim_{t \\to 0}{\\exp(\\dfrac{1}{f(a)}\\dfrac{f(a+t)-f(a)}{t})}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">根据导数定义：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$= \\exp(\\dfrac{f'(a)}{f(a)})$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-265-绝对值函数的导数\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#265-绝对值函数的导数\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.6.5 绝对值函数的导数</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">去绝对值常用方法：极限的保号性</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">左右导数存在且相等，引起符号 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to {x_0^+}}(x-x_0)=0^+, \\lim_{x \\to {x_0^-}}(x-x_0)=0^-$</math-renderer> 的符号问题，配合绝对值引起的符号问题</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 处可导，证明：若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a) = 0$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert f(x) \\rvert$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x=a$</math-renderer> 处可导的充要条件是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(a) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$(\\lvert f(x) \\rvert)'<em>{a^+} = \\lim</em>{x \\to a^+}{\\dfrac{\\lvert f(x) \\rvert}{x-a}} = \\lim_{x \\to a^+}\\lvert {\\dfrac{f(x)}{x-a}} \\rvert = \\lvert f'(a) \\rvert$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$(\\lvert f(x) \\rvert)'<em>{a^-} = \\lim</em>{x \\to a^-}{\\dfrac{\\lvert f(x) \\rvert}{x-a}} = -\\lim_{x \\to a^-}\\lvert {\\dfrac{f(x)}{x-a}} \\rvert = -\\lvert f'(a) \\rvert$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$(\\lvert f(x) \\rvert)'<em>a$ 存在 &lt;=&gt; $(\\lvert f(x) \\rvert)'</em>{a^+} = (\\lvert f(x) \\rvert)'_{a^-}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert f'(a) \\rvert = -\\lvert f'(a) \\rvert \\Rightarrow f'(a) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 处可导 &lt;=&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(a) = \\lim_{x \\to a}{\\dfrac{f(x)-f(a)}{x-a}} = \\lim_{x \\to a}{\\dfrac{f(x)}{x-a}}$</math-renderer> 存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert f(x) \\rvert$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x=a$</math-renderer> 处可导 &lt;=&gt; $(\\lvert f(x) \\rvert)'<em>a = \\lim</em>{x \\to a}{\\dfrac{\\lvert f(x) \\rvert - \\lvert f(a)\\rvert}{x-a}} = \\lim_{x \\to a}{\\dfrac{\\lvert f(x) \\rvert}{x-a}}$ 存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">我一开始以为如果 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to a}{\\dfrac{f(x)}{x-a}}$</math-renderer> 存在就必然有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to a}{\\dfrac{\\lvert f(x) \\rvert}{x-a}}$</math-renderer> 存在，毕竟只是差了一个绝对值嘛</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是实际上不能这么想，应该看的是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(a), \\lvert f'(a) \\rvert, (\\lvert f(x) \\rvert)'_a$</math-renderer> 这些整体之间的联系</p>\n</blockquote>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例 2：若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 处可导，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x_0) = a,f'(x_0) = b$</math-renderer>，而 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert f(x) \\rvert$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 处不可导，则（）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">A. a = 0, b = 0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">B. a = 0, b <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ne$</math-renderer> 0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">C. a <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ne$</math-renderer> 0, b = 0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">D. a <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ne$</math-renderer> 0, b <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ne$</math-renderer> 0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：B</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 处可导且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x_0) \\ne 0$</math-renderer>，根据复合函数求导法则：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(\\lvert f(x) \\rvert)'\\vert_{x = x_0} = (\\sqrt{f^2(x)})'\\vert_{x = x_0} = \\dfrac{2f(x)f'(x)}{2\\sqrt{f^2(x)}}\\vert_{x = x_0} = \\dfrac{f(x_0)f'(x_0)}{\\lvert f(x_0)\\rvert}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因此，$f(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 处可导，而 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert f(x) \\rvert$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 处不可导时，应有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x_0) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同时，见上题，使用左右极限也可以得出，$\\lvert f(x) \\rvert$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 处不可导时，有充要条件 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x_0) \\ne 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">注意这个 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert x \\rvert = \\sqrt{x^2}$</math-renderer> 的变形，用来去掉绝对值符号……完全没想到</p>\n</blockquote>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-27-导数应用\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#27-导数应用\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.7 导数应用</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：单调性 极值与最值 凹凸性与拐点 渐近线 曲率与曲率半径</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-271-拐点\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#271-拐点\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.7.1 拐点</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">拐点是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y''(x) = 0$</math-renderer> 的根及 <strong><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y''(x)$</math-renderer> 不存在但是函数有意义的点</strong></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-272-渐近线的求法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#272-渐近线的求法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.7.2 渐近线的求法</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">水平渐近线</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to +\\infty}f(x) = b$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=b$</math-renderer> 是一条水平渐近线</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">铅直渐近线</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to {x_0}^-}f(x) = \\infty$</math-renderer> 或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to {x_0}^+}f(x) = \\infty$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = x_0$</math-renderer> 是一条铅直渐近线</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">一般由观察法得，如分母为 0 处，对数的真数为 0 处</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">斜渐近线</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to +\\infty}\\dfrac{f(x)}{x} = a, \\lim_{x \\to +\\infty}(f(x) - ax) = b$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = ax+b$</math-renderer> 是一条斜渐近线</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to -\\infty}$</math-renderer> 同理</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-273-曲率与曲率半径\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#273-曲率与曲率半径\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.7.3 曲率与曲率半径</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 存在二阶导数，曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=f(x)$</math-renderer> 在其上点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x, f(x))$</math-renderer> 处的曲率计算公式为</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$k = \\dfrac{\\lvert f(x) \\rvert}{(1+{y'}^2)^{3/2}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">曲率半径 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$R = 1/k$</math-renderer></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">一般题目给个曲率再给个切线斜率就可以了</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同时可以根据圆心和切点的相对位置得出曲线的凹凸性，确定参数范围</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">比如抛物线的切线圆在抛物线的内部，根据相对位置可以看出 a 的正负，切点在对称轴的左边还是右边</p>\n</blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当曲线以极坐标形式给出时，为求曲线的某条切线的斜率，一般利用直角坐标与极坐标之间的关系，将曲线的极坐标方程转化为参数方程，再求切线的斜率</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">特别注意：$r'(\\theta_0)$ 不是曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r = r(\\theta)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\theta = \\theta_0$</math-renderer> 对应点处的切线斜率</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-274-由方程确定的隐函数求其驻点极值点\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#274-由方程确定的隐函数求其驻点极值点\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.7.4 由方程确定的隐函数求其驻点、极值点</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">按照隐函数的求导法则，求出导数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y'$</math-renderer> 的用 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y$</math-renderer> 表达的关系式</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y' = 0$</math-renderer> 与原方程联立，求出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y$</math-renderer> 的值</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">将求得的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y$</math-renderer> 的值代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y'$</math-renderer> 的表达式的分母（如果有的话），验算分母不为 0，则求得的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y$</math-renderer> 的值即为驻点</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y''$</math-renderer> 的表达式，代入驻点处的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x, y, y'$</math-renderer>，根据求得的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y''$</math-renderer> 的符号判断驻点是极大值还是极小值，还是不能确定</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-275-变化率与相关变化率\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#275-变化率与相关变化率\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.7.5 变化率与相关变化率</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">在某一变化过程中，涉及多个变量，如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x,y$</math-renderer> 等，如果这几个变量之间存在某种相互依赖关系，而它们又都是另一个变量 t 的可导函数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">则这几个变量以及 t 之间存在等式关系，这种关系称为相关变化率</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解决相关变化率问题时，应先建立这几个变量之间的等式关系，再用复合函数的链式法则对 t 求导</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-28-中值定理\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#28-中值定理\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.8 中值定理</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：费马定理 罗尔定理 拉格朗日中值定理 柯西中值定理 泰勒定理</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">各定理的定义：</p>\n<table>\n<thead>\n<tr>\n<th align=\"center\">定理</th>\n<th align=\"center\">条件</th>\n<th align=\"center\">内容</th>\n<th align=\"center\">用途</th>\n</tr>\n</thead>\n<tbody>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">费马定理<br>极值必要条件</td>\n<td align=\"center\">\n<math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 邻域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$U(x_0)$</math-renderer> 内有定义</td>\n<td align=\"center\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x_0)$</math-renderer> 是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 的极值，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x_0)$</math-renderer> 存在，则<br><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x_0) = 0$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">罗尔定理</td>\n<td align=\"center\">\n<math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上连续，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内可导</td>\n<td align=\"center\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a) = f(b)$</math-renderer>，则至少存在一点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 使<br><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(\\xi) = 0$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">拉格朗日中值定理<br>形式 1</td>\n<td align=\"center\">\n<math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上连续，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内可导</td>\n<td align=\"center\">至少存在一点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 使<br><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(b) - f(a) = f'(\\xi)(b-a)$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">形式 2</td>\n<td align=\"center\">同上</td>\n<td align=\"center\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x, x_0$</math-renderer> 是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上两点，则至少存在一点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 使<br><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = f(x_0)+f'(\\xi)(x-x_0)$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">形式 3</td>\n<td align=\"center\">同上</td>\n<td align=\"center\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\theta = \\dfrac{\\xi - x_0}{x-x_0}, 0&amp;lt;\\theta&amp;lt;1$</math-renderer>，形式 2 可写为<br><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = f(x_0)+f'(x_0 + \\theta(x-x_0))(x-x_0)$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">柯西中值定理</td>\n<td align=\"center\">\n<math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x), g(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上连续，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内可导，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g'(x) \\ne 0, x \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\">至少存在一点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 使<br><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{f(b)-f(a)}{g(b)-g(a)}=\\dfrac{f'(\\xi)}{g'(\\xi)}$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">泰勒定理</td>\n<td align=\"center\">根据余项的不同而不同</td>\n<td align=\"center\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x, x_0$</math-renderer> 是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上两点，则至少存在一点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 使<br><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = f(x_0) + \\dfrac{f'(x_0)}{1!}(x-x_0) + \\dfrac{f''(x_0)}{2!}(x-x_0)^2 + ... + \\dfrac{f^{(n)}(x_0)}{n!}(x-x_0)^n + R_n(x)$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">拉格朗日余项</td>\n<td align=\"center\">\n<math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上有 n 阶连续的导数，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 上有 n+1 阶导数</td>\n<td align=\"center\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$R_n(x) = \\dfrac{f^{(n+1)}(\\xi)}{(n+1)!}(x-x_0)^{n+1}$</math-renderer></td>\n<td align=\"center\">可用于区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上，例如证明不等式或等式</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">佩亚诺余项</td>\n<td align=\"center\">\n<math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上有 n 阶连续的导数，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 上有 n 阶导数</td>\n<td align=\"center\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$R_n(x) = o((x-x_0)^n)$</math-renderer></td>\n<td align=\"center\">仅能用于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 邻域，例如讨论极值及求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x \\rightarrow x_0$</math-renderer> 时的极限</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody>\n</table>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-281-罗尔定理\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#281-罗尔定理\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.8.1 罗尔定理</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.几何意义</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内有水平切线</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.证明题解题思路</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/blob/master/AdvMath/Rolle's-theorem.png\"><img src=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/raw/master/AdvMath/Rolle's-theorem.png\" height=\"200\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"></a></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>3.罗尔原话</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">假设以下提到的导数存在，有结论：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 至多有 k 个零点，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 至多有 k + 1 个零点（k = 0, 1, 2...）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">类似地，如果 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x)$</math-renderer> 至多有 k 个零点，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 至多有 k + 1 个零点，$f(x)$ 至多有 k + 2 个零点（k = 0, 1, 2...）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">以此类推</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 时，若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f^{(k)}(x) \\ne 0$</math-renderer> 恒成立（$f^{(k)}(x)$ 至多有 0 个零点），则在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 至多有 k 个零点</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)=xe^{2x}-2x-\\cos{x}$</math-renderer>，讨论它在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(-\\infty,+\\infty)$</math-renderer> 上零点的个数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">先划分区间，由连续函数介值定理讨论 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> <strong>至少</strong>有几个零点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">再根据罗尔原话确定<strong>至多</strong>有几个零点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">最终夹逼得到零点个数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(-1) = -e^{-2}+2-cos1&amp;gt;0,f(0)=-1&amp;lt;0,f(1)=e^2-2-cos1&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(-1,0)$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(0,1)$</math-renderer> 上分别至少有 1 个零点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x) = (1+2x)e^{2x}-2+\\sin{x}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">易知在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(-\\infty,-1)$</math-renderer> 上 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)&amp;lt;0$</math-renderer>，因此 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 单调递减，但 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(-1)&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer>，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(-\\infty,-1)$</math-renderer> 上没有零点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(1,+\\infty)$</math-renderer> 同理没有零点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x) = (4x+4)e^{2x}+\\cos{x}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">易知在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(-1,1)$</math-renderer> 上 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x)&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer>，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(-1,1)$</math-renderer> 内至多有两个零点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">综上，$f(x)$ 有两个零点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>4.辅助函数</strong></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(uv)' = u'v+uv'$</math-renderer> 两项加法考虑乘</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(\\dfrac{u}{v})' = \\dfrac{uv'-v'u}{v^2} \\Rightarrow f(x) = 0$</math-renderer> 两项减法考虑除</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[x^nf(x)]' = nx^{n-1}f(x)+x^nf'(x) = 0 \\Rightarrow nf(x)+xf'(x) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[e^{\\pm \\lambda x}f(x)]' = \\pm \\lambda e^{\\pm \\lambda x} f(x) + e^{\\pm \\lambda x}f'(x) = 0 \\Rightarrow \\pm \\lambda f(x) + f'(x) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">乘以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x^n$</math-renderer> 或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$e^{\\pm \\lambda x}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">作差构造辅助函数，例如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) = f(x) - y_{\\overline{AB}}(x)$</math-renderer> 表示函数与区间端点连线的所在直线的函数之间的差值</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">在需证明的等式两端同时加、减某一函数</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因为题目一般给出的关系式是包括了 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'$</math-renderer>，所以可以考虑能否华为分离变量的微分方程或者解微分方程</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">使用对数函数特性</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设常数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer>，讨论 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a$</math-renderer> 的值，确定曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=e^{ax}$</math-renderer> 与曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=x^2$</math-renderer> 在第一象限中公共点的个数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$e^{ax} = x^2$</math-renderer> 两边去对数后得到 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$ax = 2\\ln{x}$</math-renderer> 方便讨论</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令某一参数为变量</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：要证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a,b) &amp;lt; g(a,b)$</math-renderer>，可以构造 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(x) = f(a,x) - g(a,x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是有些构造就真的很天马行空了……积分也积不出</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,1]$</math-renderer> 上二阶可导，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0) = 0,f(1) = 1$</math-renderer>，求证：存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\in (0,1)$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi f''(\\xi)+(1+\\xi)f'(\\xi) = 1+\\xi$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">构造：$F(x) = e^xx(f'(x)-1)$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求导得 $F'(x) = e^x[x(f'(x)-1)]+e^x(f'(x)-1)+e^xxf''(x) \\\n= e^x[xf''(x)+(1+x)f'(x)-(1+x)]$</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-282-拉格朗日中值定理\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#282-拉格朗日中值定理\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.8.2 拉格朗日中值定理</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.几何意义</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内存在与端点连线平行的切线</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.证明题解题思路</strong></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">“增量”</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(b)-f(a) = f'(\\xi)(b-a),\\xi in (a,b)$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">“表达”</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = f(x_0) + f'(\\xi)(x - x_0)$</math-renderer>，$\\xi in (x_0,x)$ 或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi in (x,x_0)$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">不同函数在同一区间上用拉格朗日中值定理</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同一函数在不同区间上用拉格朗日中值定理</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用 $f(b)-f(a) = f'<a href=\"b-a\">a+\\theta(b-a)</a><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$，求 $</math-renderer>\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\theta(x)$ 等</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例题：凑成“增量”形式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(b) - f(a)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to \\infty}{x(\\dfrac{\\pi}{4}-\\arctan{\\dfrac{x}{1+x}})}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">实际上是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\arctan1$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\arctan{\\dfrac{x}{1+x}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$b=1,a=\\dfrac{x}{1+x}\\rightarrow 1$</math-renderer>，这样夹逼 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\rightarrow 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-283-双中值问题\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#283-双中值问题\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.8.3 双中值问题</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证明思路 1：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">不同函数在同一区间上用拉格朗日中值定理</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同一函数在不同区间上用拉格朗日中值定理（划分区间）</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">综合应用柯西中值定理与拉格朗日中值定理或泰勒公式</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证明思路 2：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即有两个值 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\eta$</math-renderer>，分离 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\eta$</math-renderer>，两边都使用一次中值定理</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">不要求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi\\neq\\eta$</math-renderer>，对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a,b$</math-renderer> 使用两次中值定理，要么两次拉格朗日中值定理，要么一次拉格朗日中值定理一次柯西中值定理</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">要求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi\\neq\\eta$</math-renderer>，找点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$c$</math-renderer>，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,c)$</math-renderer>、$c,b$ 区间上分别使用两次拉格朗日中值定理或一次拉格朗日中值定理一次柯西中值定理</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$c$</math-renderer> 的取值，要么是第一问给出，要么逆推假设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$c$</math-renderer> 已知根据要证的结论推出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$c$</math-renderer>（基本上不会考到）</p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">感觉看上去都很厉害……当然还是要做题才能理解</p>\n</blockquote>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\"
