data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在闭区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,c]$</math-renderer> 上连续，其导数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 在开区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(0,c)$</math-renderer> 内存在且单调减少，又 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0)=0$</math-renderer>，证明 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a+b)\\leqslant f(a)+f(b)$</math-renderer>，$0\\leqslant a\\leqslant b\\leqslant a+b\\leqslant c$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：不存在两端点相等的条件，所以使用拉格朗日中值定理</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因为所要证明的式子中含有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a$</math-renderer>、$b$、$a+b$，$f(0)=0$，所以对这几个区间进行拉格朗日中值定理。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证明式子中没有减的形式只有和的形式，所以需要对其转换</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第一次转换：要证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a+b) - f(b)\\leqslant f(a)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这时可以对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a+b) - f(b)$</math-renderer> 做一次拉格朗日中值定理 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a+b)-f(b)=f'(\\xi_1)(a+b-b) = f'(\\xi_1)a$</math-renderer>，$b &lt; \\xi_1 &lt; a+b$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(\\xi_1)a \\leqslant f(a)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第二次转换：要证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(\\xi_1) \\leqslant \\dfrac{f(a)-0}{a-0} = \\dfrac{f(a)-f(0)}{a-0}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这时可以对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a)-f(0)$</math-renderer> 做一次拉格朗日中值定理 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a)-f(0)=f'(\\xi_2)(a-0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(\\xi_1) \\leqslant f'(\\xi_2)$</math-renderer>，$0&lt;\\xi_2&lt;a&lt;b&lt;\\xi_1&lt;a+b$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)$</math-renderer> 单调减少，所以自然有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(\\xi_1)&amp;lt;f'(\\xi_2)$</math-renderer> 即原命题得证</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证明存在两个不同的点在同一个区间满足一个不等式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果两个点彼此存在一定关系，如上面式子转换的例子 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a+b$</math-renderer>，$a$，$b$，那么我们可以使用转换</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果两个完全独立的变量，则这种方式没用</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">我们可以考虑划分区间，假定这两个点在不同的区间，中间以一个区间变量分隔</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于拉格朗日中值定理中两个变量只会出现一次，而间隔变量会出现多次</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以对其分别拉格朗日中值定理，就可以把两个变量换成以间隔变量表示的形式，将两个无关变量的式子变成一个变量的式子</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,1]$</math-renderer> 上连续，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(0,1)$</math-renderer> 内可导，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0)=0$</math-renderer>，$f(1)=1$，证明存在不同的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_1$</math-renderer>、$\\xi_2$，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{f'(\\xi_1)}+\\dfrac{1}{f'(\\xi_2)}=2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证明：使用 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi$</math-renderer> 将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,1]$</math-renderer> 划分为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,\\xi]$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[\\xi,1]$</math-renderer> 两个区间，假定 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_1$</math-renderer>、$\\xi_2$ 分别在这两个区间上</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">分别对其进行拉格朗日：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(\\xi)-f(0)=f'(\\xi_1)(\\xi-0)$</math-renderer>，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{f'(\\xi_1)}=\\dfrac{\\xi}{f(\\xi)}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(1)-f(\\xi)=f'(\\xi_2)(1-\\xi)$</math-renderer>，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{f'(\\xi_2)}=\\dfrac{1-\\xi}{1-f(\\xi)}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{f'(\\xi_1)}+\\dfrac{1}{f'(\\xi_2)}=\\dfrac{\\xi}{f(\\xi)}+\\dfrac{1-\\xi}{1-f(\\xi)}$</math-renderer>，任取$f(\\xi)=\\dfrac{1}{2}$，原式等于2，得证</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在闭区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,1]$</math-renderer> 上连续，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I = \\int_0^1f(x)dx \\ne 0$</math-renderer>，证明：在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(0,1)$</math-renderer> 内存在不同的两点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_1,\\xi_2$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{f(\\xi_1)}+\\dfrac{1}{f(\\xi_2)} = \\dfrac{2}{I}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证明：使用 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi$</math-renderer> 将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,1]$</math-renderer> 划分为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,\\xi]$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[\\xi,1]$</math-renderer> 两个区间，假定 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_1$</math-renderer>、$\\xi_2$ 分别在这两个区间上</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) = \\dfrac{1}{I}\\int_0^xf(t)dt$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(0) = 0, F(1) = 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(\\xi)-F(0)=F'(\\xi_1)(\\xi-0)=\\dfrac{1}{I}f(\\xi_1)\\xi$</math-renderer>，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(\\xi)=\\dfrac{1}{I}f(\\xi_1)\\xi$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(1)-F(\\xi)=F'(\\xi_2)(1-\\xi)=\\dfrac{1}{I}f(\\xi_2)(1-\\xi)$</math-renderer>，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$1-F(\\xi)=\\dfrac{1}{I}f(\\xi_2)(1-\\xi)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">任取 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi$</math-renderer> 使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(\\xi) = \\dfrac{1}{2}$</math-renderer>，有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{2}=\\dfrac{1}{I}f(\\xi_1)\\xi \\Rightarrow \\dfrac{1}{f(\\xi_1)} = \\dfrac{2}{I}\\xi$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{2}=\\dfrac{1}{I}f(\\xi_2)(1-\\xi) \\Rightarrow \\dfrac{1}{f(\\xi_2)} = \\dfrac{2}{I}(1-\\xi)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{f(\\xi_1)}+\\dfrac{1}{f(\\xi_2)} = \\dfrac{2}{I}\\xi + \\dfrac{2}{I}(1-\\xi) = \\dfrac{2}{I}$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-284-柯西中值定理\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#284-柯西中值定理\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.8.4 柯西中值定理</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.几何意义</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由参数方程表示的曲线在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内存在切线与端点的连线是平行的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.证明题解题思路</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">凑成形式</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-285-泰勒公式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#285-泰勒公式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.8.5 泰勒公式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">常用拉格朗日余项的泰勒公式证明不等式</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">展开的阶数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n$</math-renderer> 阶可导则只展开到 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n-1$</math-renderer> 阶，第 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n$</math-renderer> 阶留给余项</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">只要给出二阶或二阶以上可导，可以先泰勒展开看看</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">展开点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">把 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在给定信息最多的点上泰勒展开</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若两点信息一样多，则优先在有导数信息的一点展开</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若两点都是导数信息或函数信息，则对两点分别展开</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">消去式中某阶导数的方法</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">取极值点消去一阶导，取驻点消去二阶导</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">将一些已知数据代入，利用加减将这项消除</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内存在二阶导数，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x) &amp;lt; 0$</math-renderer>，试证明：对于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内的任意两个不同的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_1$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_2$</math-renderer>，以及满足 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$s+t=1,0&amp;lt;s&amp;lt;1$</math-renderer> 的两个数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$s$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t$</math-renderer>，均有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(sx_1+tx_2)&amp;gt;sf(x_1)+tf(x_2)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">题目给出 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x)$</math-renderer> 存在且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x)$</math-renderer> 具有一定的符号，要证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 满足某不等式，一般想到将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在某点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = x_0$</math-renderer> 处按拉格朗日余项的泰勒公式展开至 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n = 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = f(x_0) + f'(x_0)(x-x_0)+\\dfrac{1}{2!}f''(\\xi)(x-x_0)^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中，自然利用已知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x)$</math-renderer> 的符号，将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(\\xi)$</math-renderer> 抹去成为一个不等式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">将该式与题目对照，式中不能含有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x_0)$</math-renderer>，如何消除？通过加减</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当然，看到二阶导数也可以想到使用两次中值定理，但是这或许有点需要技巧……</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">法 1：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">泰勒展开</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = f(x_0) + f'(x_0)(x-x_0)+\\dfrac{1}{2!}f''(\\xi)(x-x_0)^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">分别代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = x_1, x = x_2$</math-renderer>，得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x_1) = f(x_0) + f'(x_0)(x_1-x_0)+\\dfrac{1}{2!}f''(\\xi)(x_1-x_0)^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x_2) = f(x_0) + f'(x_0)(x_2-x_0)+\\dfrac{1}{2!}f''(\\xi)(x_2-x_0)^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第一式乘 s，第二式乘 t，相加：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$sf(x_1)+tf(x_2) = f(x_0) + f'(x_0)(sx_1+tx_2-x_0)+\\dfrac{s}{2!}f''(\\xi)(x_1-x_0)^2+\\dfrac{t}{2!}f''(\\xi)(x_2-x_0)^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x) &amp;lt; 0$</math-renderer>，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(\\xi) &amp;lt; 0$</math-renderer>，所以</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$sf(x_1)+tf(x_2) &amp;lt; f(x_0) + f'(x_0)(sx_1+tx_2-x_0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0 = sx_1+tx_2$</math-renderer>，得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$sf(x_1)+tf(x_2) &amp;lt; f(sx_1+tx_2)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">法 2：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\nf(sx_1+tx_2)-sf(x_1)-tf(x_2) = (s+t)f(sx_1+tx_2)-sf(x_1)-tf(x_2) \\\n= s[f(sx_1+tx_2)-f(x_1)]+t[f(sx_1+tx_2)-f(x_2)] \\\n= sf'(\\xi_1)[(s-1)x_1+tx_2]+tf'(\\xi_2)[sx_1+(t-1)x_2] \\\n= stf'(\\xi_1)(x_2-x_1)-stf'(\\xi_2)(x_2-x_1) \\\n= stf''(\\xi_3)(\\xi_1-\\xi_2)(x_2-x_1)\n$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(\\xi_3) &amp;lt; 0, \\xi_1-\\xi_2 &amp;lt; 0, x_2 - x_1 &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer>，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$stf''(\\xi_3)(\\xi_1-\\xi_2)(x_2-x_1) &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 $f(sx_1+tx_2)-sf(x_1)-tf(x_2) &gt; 0</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-286-零点存在性\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#286-零点存在性\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.8.6 零点存在性</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">连续函数介值定理</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">罗尔定理</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其他</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上可导，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(a)f'(b)&amp;lt;0$</math-renderer>，证明至少存在一点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(\\xi) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这里的条件是“$f(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上可导”而不是“$f‘(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上连续”，所以不能用介值定理</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">不妨认为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(a)&amp;lt;0,f'(b)&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer>，从而有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to a^+}\\dfrac{f(x)-f(a)}{x-a} = f'(a) &amp;lt; 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to b^-}\\dfrac{f(x)-f(b)}{x-b} = f'(b) &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由保号性知，存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\delta_1 &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer>，当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0&amp;lt;x-a&amp;lt;\\delta_1$</math-renderer> 时，$f(x)-f(a)&lt;0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同理，存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\delta_2 &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer>，当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$-\\delta_2&amp;lt;x-b&amp;lt;0$</math-renderer> 时，$f(x)-f(b)&lt;0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">从而知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a),f(b)$</math-renderer> 都不是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上的最小值</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">故 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 的最小值点必在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 的内部，它必然是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 的极小值点</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-287-实系数奇次方程\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#287-实系数奇次方程\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.8.7 实系数奇次方程</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">实系数奇次方程至少有一个实根。即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x^{2n+1}+a_1x^{2n}+\\cdots+a_{2n}x+a_{2n+1}=0$</math-renderer> 至少有一个实根</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这个判断法则往往要和罗尔原话一起使用确定是否有且仅有常数个实根</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\">\n<a id=\"user-content-288-证明存在某-xi-满足某不等式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#288-%E8%AF%81%E6%98%8E%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E6%9F%90-xi-%E6%BB%A1%E8%B6%B3%E6%9F%90%E4%B8%8D%E7%AD%89%E5%BC%8F\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.8.8 证明存在某 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi$</math-renderer> 满足某不等式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证明不等式：证明不等式在某区间成立</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">满足不等式：证明不等式在某区间的某一点上成立</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">零点问题：证明等式在某区间的某一点上成立</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上连续，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b)$</math-renderer> 内可导，并且不是一次式，证明至少存在一点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi$</math-renderer> 使 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert f'(\\xi) \\rvert &amp;gt; \\lvert \\dfrac{f(b)-f(a)}{b-a} \\rvert$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>描述函数不是一次式的方法：</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设点 A <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,f(a))$</math-renderer>，点 B <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(b,f(b))$</math-renderer>，考虑曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=f(x)$</math-renderer> 的弧 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\overset{\\frown}{AB}$</math-renderer> 的纵坐标与弦 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\overline{AB}$</math-renderer> 的纵坐标的差</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(x) = f(x) - [f(a) + \\dfrac{f(b)-f(a)}{b-a}(x-a)] \\not\\equiv 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又因为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(a) = \\varphi(b) = 0$</math-renderer>，所以至少存在一点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_1 \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(x_1)&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer> 或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(x_1)&amp;lt;0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">之后移项用一次拉格朗日中值定理就好了</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-29-常用结论\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#29-常用结论\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.9 常用结论</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-291-复杂式子求值可以尝试用等价无穷小化简\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#291-复杂式子求值可以尝试用等价无穷小化简\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>2.9.1 复杂式子求值可以尝试用等价无穷小化简</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">学到等价无穷小的时候，我不知道别人是否跟我一样，觉得这东西完全可以用泰勒公式取代</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当然是这样的，当然可以用泰勒取代</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是重要的是思想，就是说，当你看到一个复杂的式子的时候，你有两个选择，一个选择是把这个解析式展开，另一个选择是化简</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果你对是否化简不能确定，或者说你不知道怎么化简的时候，你就会想，是不是需要展开？但是展开又太难</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">之后就会陷入自我怀疑的深渊……</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">实际上泰勒展开肯定是没错！但是展开会写得很长！</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以说，需要确立一个使用等价无穷小化简的思路，在看到题目的时候立即这样想，之后再尝试用泰勒之类的，也就会自然而然地用出来</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = f(x)$</math-renderer> 有二阶导数，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x) &amp;gt; 0, f(x) = 0, f'(x) = 0$</math-renderer>，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{x^3f(u)}{f(x)\\sin^3{u}}$</math-renderer>，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$u$</math-renderer> 是曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = f(x)$</math-renderer> 上点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$p(x,f(x))$</math-renderer> 处的切线在 x 轴上的截距</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">易得：$u = x - \\dfrac{f(x)}{f'(x)}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果这个时候要把 u 代入式子，然后研究这个式子的性质，就会觉得很难</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以这个时候要相信可以化简，怎么化简？都趋于 0 了，用等价无穷小咯</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由泰勒：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = 0 + 0 + \\dfrac{1}{2}f''(0)x^2 + o(x^2)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(u) = 0 + 0 + \\dfrac{1}{2}f''(0)u^2 + o(u^2)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由等价无穷小：$\\sin^3{u} \\sim u^3$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{x^3f(u)}{f(x)\\sin^3{u}} = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{x^3}{u^3}\\dfrac{\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(0)u^2 + o(u^2)}{\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(0)x^2 + o(x^2)} = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{x}{u} = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{x}{x - \\dfrac{f(x)}{f'(x)}} = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{1}{1 - \\dfrac{f(x)}{xf'(x)}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}1 - \\dfrac{f(x)}{xf'(x)} = 1-\\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{f(x)}{xf'(x)}} = 1-\\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(0)x^2 + o(x^2)}{xf'(x)}} = 1-\\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(0) + o(1)}{\\dfrac{f'(x)}{x}}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又因为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x) = 0$</math-renderer> 有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$1-\\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(0) + o(1)}{\\dfrac{f'(x)}{x}}} = 1-\\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(0) + o(1)}{\\dfrac{f'(x) - f'(0)}{x-0}}} = 1-\\lim_{x \\to 0}{\\dfrac{\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(0) + o(1)}{f''(0)}} = 1-\\dfrac{1}{2} = \\dfrac{1}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{x^3f(u)}{f(x)\\sin^3{u}} = 2$</math-renderer></p>\n<h2 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-第三章-一元函数积分学\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#第三章-一元函数积分学\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>第三章 一元函数积分学</h2>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-31-不定积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#31-不定积分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.1 不定积分</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：定义 性质 计算方法</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-311-奇偶函数周期函数的原函数与变限积分的对比\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#311-奇偶函数周期函数的原函数与变限积分的对比\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.1.1 奇、偶函数，周期函数的原函数与变限积分的对比</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由原函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x)$</math-renderer> 的奇偶性、周期性推断 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 的相应性质，用到微分学的知识</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 的奇偶性、周期性推断原函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x)$</math-renderer> 的相应性质，自然用到积分学</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是不是不定积分，不定积分只能用来作为运算，不能用来讨论性质</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">应该用变上限函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^x{f(t)dt}$</math-renderer> 来表示 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 的某一个原函数，用它来讨论原函数的性质</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即：</p>\n<table>\n<thead>\n<tr>\n<th align=\"center\"></th>\n<th align=\"center\"></th>\n</tr>\n</thead>\n<tbody>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">从 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 到 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x)$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = F'(x), f(-x) = F'(-x)$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">从 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x)$</math-renderer> 到 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) + C = \\int_0^x{f(u)du}, F(-x) + C = \\int_0^{-x}{f(u)du}$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n</tr>\n</tbody>\n</table>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-312-换元法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#312-换元法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.1.2 换元法</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.第一类换元</strong></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">凑微分法</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">积化和差 和差化积</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">三角等式</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">反三角换元</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">指对换元</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">倒数换元</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有理换元</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">万能公式</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.第二类换元</strong></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int{R(x,\\sqrt{a^2-x^2})dx},\\int{R(x,\\sqrt{x^2 \\pm a^2})dx}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">三角换元</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当被积函数含有根式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sqrt{ax^2+bx+c}$</math-renderer> 时，需要对其配方变成 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sqrt{\\varphi^2(x)+k^2}$</math-renderer>、$\\sqrt{\\varphi^2(x)-k^2}$、$\\sqrt{k^2-\\varphi^2(x)}$ 三种形式再进行三角换元</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int{R(x,\\sqrt[n]{ax+b},\\sqrt[m]{ax+b})dx}$</math-renderer>，$a \\ne 0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t = \\sqrt[nm]{ax+b}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int{R(x,\\sqrt{\\dfrac{ax+b}{cx+d}})dx}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t = \\sqrt{\\dfrac{ax+b}{cx+d}}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int{R(\\sin{x},\\cos{x})dx}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">万能公式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t = \\tan{\\dfrac{x}{2}}$</math-renderer> 萬不得已再用</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>3.辅助换元</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">在使用换元法的时候有可能单个式子不能求出积分，而使用其他辅助式子加减在一起积分可以得到结果，从而能得到原式和辅助式子的积分结果。对于这类题目需要观察什么样的式子能让积分简单</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}x}{x+\\sqrt{1-x^2}}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x=\\sin t$</math-renderer>，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sqrt{1-x^2}=\\cos t$</math-renderer>，$\\textrm{d}x=\\cos t,\\textrm{d}t$。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\because x+\\sqrt{1-x^2}$</math-renderer> 可能为正可能为负，正负时单调性不同，所以令 $ x+\\sqrt{1-x^2}=0$，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin t=-\\dfrac{\\sqrt{2}}{2}$</math-renderer>，从而 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t\\in(-\\dfrac{\\pi}{2},-\\dfrac{\\pi}{4})\\cup(-\\dfrac{\\pi}{4},\\dfrac{\\pi}{2})$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\therefore=\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{\\cos t}{\\sin t+\\cos t}\\textrm{d}t}$</math-renderer>（$t\\in(-\\dfrac{\\pi}{4},\\dfrac{\\pi}{2})$）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这时你会发现使用积化和差、万能公式、倍角公式都无法解出这个积分，所以这时候就需要另外一个辅助积分式子加上或减去这个式子，从而让和以及差更容易解出积分。这里根据式子特点让辅助式子分子为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin t$</math-renderer>：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1=\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{\\cos t}{\\sin t+\\cos t}\\textrm{d}t}$</math-renderer>，$I_2=\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{\\sin t}{\\sin t+\\cos t}\\textrm{d}t}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1+I_2=\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{\\sin t+\\cos t}{\\sin t+\\cos t}\\textrm{d}t=\\int\\textrm{d}t=t}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1-I_2=\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{\\cos t-\\sin t}{\\sin t+\\cos t}\\textrm{d}t=\\int\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}(\\sin t+\\cos t)}{\\sin t+\\cos t}}=\\ln\\vert\\sin t+\\cos t\\vert +C$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1=\\dfrac{1}{2}(\\arcsin x+\\ln\\vert x+\\sqrt{1-x^2}\\vert)+C$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同理 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t\\in(-\\dfrac{\\pi}{2},-\\dfrac{\\pi}{4})$</math-renderer>也得到同样结果</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-313-分部积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#313-分部积分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.1.3 分部积分</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.非幂函数优先</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当幂函数与一些微分后能降低幂函数幂次的函数在一起时，先对非幂函数优先分部积分，结果与幂函数相乘可以消去幂次，以达到降低幂次的作用</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int x^n\\ln x,\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer>，$\\int x^n\\arctan x,\\textrm{d}x$，$\\int x^n\\arcsin x,\\textrm{d}x$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.幂函数优先</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当幂函数与三角函数在一起微分时，因为三角函数无论如何积分都不会被消去，所以应该优先消去幂函数部分，从而降低幂次</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int{x^n \\sin{x}dx}, \\int{x^n \\cos{x}dx}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>3.多次分部</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于一部分通过微分形式不会发生变化的函数，所以需要多次积分，然后利用等式求出目标值。即三角函数和指数函数，这两种积分形式不变，指数函数一次积分保持不变，而三角函数两次积分保持不变。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">也称为积分再现、循环积分法</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如：$\\int e^x\\sin x,\\textrm{d}x$，$\\int e^x\\cos x,\\textrm{d}x$</p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">常常<strong>交替使用换元法和分部积分</strong></p>\n</blockquote>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-314-有理积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#314-有理积分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.1.4 有理积分</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.高阶多项式分配</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当不定积分式子形如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{f(x)}{g(x)},\\textrm{d}x}$</math-renderer>，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer>、$g(x)$ 都为与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 相关的多项式，$f(x)$ 阶数高于或等于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 可以按照 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)$</math-renderer> 的形式分配，约去式子，得到最简单的表达</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.低阶多项式分解</strong>（留数拆分）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当不定积分式子形如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{f(x)}{g(x)},\\textrm{d}x}$</math-renderer>，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer>、$g(x)$ 都为与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 相关的多项式，$f(x)$ 阶数低于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)$</math-renderer> 可以因式分解为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)=g_1(x)g_2(x)\\cdots$</math-renderer> 时，先因式分解再进行运算</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">一次单项式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$ax+b$</math-renderer> 产生一项 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{A}{ax+b}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$k$</math-renderer> 重一次因式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(ax+b)^k$</math-renderer> 产生 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$k$</math-renderer> 项：$\\dfrac{A_1}{ax+b}+\\dfrac{A_2}{(ax+b)^2}+\\cdots+\\dfrac{A_n}{(ax+b)^n}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">二次因式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$px^2+qx+r$</math-renderer> 产生一项：$\\dfrac{Ax+B}{px^2+qx+r}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$k$</math-renderer> 重二次因式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(px^2+qx+r)^k$</math-renderer> 产生 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$k$</math-renderer> 项：$\\dfrac{A_1x+B_1}{px^2+qx+r}+\\cdots+\\dfrac{A_nx+B_n}{(px^2+qx+r)^k}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>3.低阶多项式分配</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当不定积分式子形如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{f(x)}{g(x)},\\textrm{d}x}$</math-renderer>，且$f(x)$、$g(x)$ 都为与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 相关的多项式，$f(x)$ 阶数低于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)$</math-renderer> 不能因式分解为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)=g_1(x)g_2(x)\\cdots$</math-renderer> 时，则可以分配式子：$\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{f(x)}{g(x)},\\textrm{d}x=a_1\\int\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}(f_1(x))}{g_1(x)}+a_2\\int\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}(f_2(x))}{g_2(x)}}+\\cdots$，将积分式子组合成积分结果为分式的函数，如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ln x$</math-renderer>、$\\arcsin x$、$\\arctan x$等</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\displaystyle{\\int\\dfrac{x-1}{x^2+2x+3}\\textrm{d}x}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：因为$x^2+2x+3$不能因式分解，所以考虑将分子按照分母形式进行分配。优先对高阶的$x$进行分配。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">首先因为分子最高阶为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 只比分母最高 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x^2$</math-renderer> 低一阶，所以考虑将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x-1$</math-renderer> 分配到微分号内。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\because\\textrm{d}(x^2+2x+3)=2x+2$</math-renderer>，而现在是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x-1$</math-renderer>，所以：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$=\\displaystyle{\\dfrac{1}{2}\\int\\dfrac{2x+2}{x^2+2x+3}\\textrm{d}x-2\\int\\dfrac{1}{x^2+2x+3}\\textrm{d}x}=\\displaystyle{\\dfrac{1}{2}\\int\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}(x^2+2x+3)}{x^2+2x+3}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">类似的有三角函数的分配：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{C\\sin{x}+D\\cos{x}}{A\\sin{x}+B\\cos{x}} = \\dfrac{h(A\\cos{x}-B\\sin{x})}{A\\sin{x}+B\\cos{x}} + \\dfrac{k(A\\sin{x}+B\\cos{x})}{A\\sin{x}+B\\cos{x}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由 $\n\\left{\n\\begin{array}{lcl}\n-Bh+Ak = C \\\nAh+Bk = D\n\\end{array}\n\\right.\n$ 解出 h 与 k</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-315-常用不定积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#315-常用不定积分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.1.5 常用不定积分</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int{\\dfrac{1}{\\sqrt{1+x^2}}dx} = \\ln(x+\\sqrt{1+x^2})+C$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">变量代换 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = \\tan{\\theta}$</math-renderer> 得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int{\\dfrac{1}{\\sqrt{1+x^2}}dx} = \\int{\\dfrac{1}{\\cos{\\theta}}d\\theta}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于分母中的三角函数是奇数次幂，容易想到变形为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int{\\dfrac{1}{\\cos{\\theta}}d\\theta} = \\int{\\dfrac{\\cos{\\theta}}{\\cos^2{\\theta}}d\\theta} = \\int{\\dfrac{\\cos{\\theta}}{1-\\sin^2{\\theta}}d\\theta}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">变量代换 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t = \\sin{\\theta}$</math-renderer> 得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int{\\dfrac{\\cos{\\theta}}{1-\\sin^2{\\theta}}d\\theta} = \\int{\\dfrac{1}{1-t^2}dt} = \\int{\\dfrac{1}{1+t}+\\dfrac{1}{1-t}dt} = \\dfrac{1}{2}\\ln \\lvert \\dfrac{1+t}{1-t} \\rvert +C = \\dfrac{1}{2}\\ln \\lvert \\dfrac{1+\\sin{\\theta}}{1-\\sin{\\theta}} \\rvert +C$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">要研究 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = \\tan{\\theta}$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin{\\theta}$</math-renderer> 之间的关系，可以设一个边长为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$1,x,\\sqrt{1+x^2}$</math-renderer> 的直角三角形，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\theta$</math-renderer> 的对边长为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer>，那么 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin{\\theta}$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 之间就可以建立联系，即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin{\\theta} = \\dfrac{x}{\\sqrt{1+x^2}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">代入得：$\\dfrac{1}{2}\\ln \\lvert\\dfrac{1+\\sin{\\theta}}{1-\\sin{\\theta}}\\rvert +C = \\dfrac{1}{2}\\ln \\lvert\\dfrac{1+\\dfrac{x}{\\sqrt{1+x^2}}}{1-\\dfrac{x}{\\sqrt{1+x^2}}}\\rvert +C = \\dfrac{1}{2}\\ln \\lvert\\dfrac{\\sqrt{1+x^2}+x}{\\sqrt{1+x^2}-x}\\rvert +C = \\dfrac{1}{2}\\ln \\lvert(\\sqrt{1+x^2}+x)^2\\rvert +C = \\ln(x+\\sqrt{1+x^2})+C$</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-32-定积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#32-定积分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.2 定积分</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：定义 性质 定理 计算方法</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-321-区间再现\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#321-区间再现\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.2.1 区间再现</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 为连续函数，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(x),\\textrm{d}x=\\int_a^bf(a+b-x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">区间再现本质是一种换元法，但是实际上是显式地根据函数周期移动 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 的范围，求出另一种形式，再结合一起解出。这种方法类似多次分部积分求出两边同一个形式的不定积分然后相减的方法</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">基本上三角函数相关的式子，如果直接求不出来就可以考虑区间再现。一般积分区间为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,a]$</math-renderer>，令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x=a-t$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同时，区间再现的区间也要考虑到式子的实际意义</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">比如要考察 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{0}^{\\pi/2}{\\dfrac{\\cos{x}-\\sin{x}}{1+x^2}}$</math-renderer> 的正负时，一般直接想到对这个式子作 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t = \\dfrac{\\pi}{2} - x$</math-renderer> 的区间再现，但做完之后就不知道怎么办了</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">考虑到式子的实际意义，由于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\cos{x}-\\sin{x}$</math-renderer> 的正负不是以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,\\dfrac{\\pi}{2}]$</math-renderer> 为划分，而是以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,\\dfrac{\\pi}{4}],[\\dfrac{\\pi}{4},\\dfrac{\\pi}{2}]$</math-renderer> 为划分</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以原式要拆成 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{0}^{\\pi/4}{\\dfrac{\\cos{x}-\\sin{x}}{1+x^2}} + \\int_{\\pi/4}^{\\pi/2}{\\dfrac{\\cos{x}-\\sin{x}}{1+x^2}}$</math-renderer> 然后对第二项作 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t = \\dfrac{\\pi}{2} - x$</math-renderer> 的区间再现</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">之后再合并，就可以发现式子的正负</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-322-定限积分等式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#322-定限积分等式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.2.2 定限积分等式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">1.函数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求函数时表达式中含有积分式子，这时可以令其为常数项，然后反代计算定积分</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.积分值</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">基本上是给出一个一个已知表达式的积分并给出积分值，然后求另一个表达式的积分值。可以令这个积分表达式为$t$代入原积分表达式，也可以将积分式子初等运算</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$f(3)$ 为连续函数，$\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}f(x\\cos x)\\cos x,\\textrm{d}x=A$，求$\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}f(x\\cos x)x\\sin x,\\textrm{d}x$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：$\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}f(x\\cos x)\\cos x,\\textrm{d}x-\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}f(x\\cos x)x\\sin x,\\textrm{d}x=\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}f(x\\cos x)(\\cos x,\\textrm{d}x+x,\\textrm{d}\\cos x)=\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}f(x\\cos x)\\textrm{d}(x\\cos x)=F(x\\cos x)\\vert_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}=F(0)-F(0)=0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\therefore\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}f(x\\cos x)\\cos x,\\textrm{d}x=\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}f(x\\cos x)x\\sin x,\\textrm{d}x=A$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-323-积分中值定理\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#323-积分中值定理\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0
