2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.2.3 积分中值定理</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">中值定理一般是在微分中使用，积分中也可能考到，但是重点是将定限积分化为两个常数的差的形式，所以基本上使用拉格朗日中值定理。</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">积分中值定理：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在$[a,b]$ 上连续，则存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi\\in[a,b]$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(x),\\textrm{d}x=f(\\xi)(b-a)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer>、$g(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上连续，$g(x)$ 不变号，则存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi\\in[a,b]$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(x)g(x),\\\\textrm{d}x=f(\\xi)\\int_a^bg(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer></p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 n 是正整数，p 是大于零的常数，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}\\dfrac{\\sin{x}}{x}dx$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}\\dfrac{\\sin{x}}{x}dx = \\dfrac{\\sin{\\xi}}{\\xi}(n+p-n) = p\\dfrac{\\sin{\\xi}}{\\xi} = p\\dfrac{1}{\\xi}\\sin{\\xi}$</math-renderer> = p·0·有界量 = 0</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-324-二重积分的积分中值定理\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#324-二重积分的积分中值定理\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.2.4 二重积分的积分中值定理</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 连续，则必存在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0) \\in D$</math-renderer>，使得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\iint_D{f(x,y)dxdy} = f(x_0,y_0)\\lvert D \\rvert$</math-renderer>，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lvert D \\rvert$</math-renderer> 表示 D 的面积</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-325-被积函数化简\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#325-被积函数化简\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.2.5 被积函数化简</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">被积函数可能看上去很复杂，或者由于被积函数中某一部分的存在，导致正常思路被堵死</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这个时候可以尝试化简掉那个导致复杂的部分</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\arcsin{x} + \\arccos{x} = \\dfrac{\\pi}{2}, -1 \\leqslant x \\leqslant 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\arctan{x} + \\arctan{\\dfrac{1}{x}} = \\dfrac{\\pi}{2}, x &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：定积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I = \\int_{-\\pi}^{\\pi}{\\dfrac{x\\sin{x}\\arctan{e^x}}{1+\\cos^2{x}}}dx$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有 x 有三角，一眼区间再现</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是有一个 arctanx 难搞，所以要消掉它</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\nI = \\int_{-\\pi}^{0}{\\dfrac{x\\sin{x}\\arctan{e^x}}{1+\\cos^2{x}}}dx + \\int_{0}^{\\pi}{\\dfrac{x\\sin{x}\\arctan{e^x}}{1+\\cos^2{x}}}dx \\\n= \\int_{0}^{\\pi}{\\dfrac{x\\sin{x}\\arctan{e^{-x}}}{1+\\cos^2{x}}}dx + \\int_{0}^{\\pi}{\\dfrac{x\\sin{x}\\arctan{e^x}}{1+\\cos^2{x}}}dx \\\n= \\dfrac{\\pi}{2}\\int_{0}^{\\pi}{\\dfrac{x\\sin{x}}{1+\\cos^2{x}}}dx \\\n$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">之后用区间再现</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-326-积分区间化简\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#326-积分区间化简\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.2.6 积分区间化简</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.利用周期性</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$\\int_0^{2n\\pi}{\\lvert \\sin{t} \\rvert dt} = 2n\\int_0^{\\pi}{\\lvert \\sin{t} \\rvert dt}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.根据题目所给条件的意义缩小积分区间</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = (x+1)(e^{nx}-1),n&amp;gt;1$</math-renderer> 与 x 轴所围面积</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果上来就求从负无穷到正无穷，那就没法求了</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">实际上，要求与 x 轴所围面积，首先要知道与 x 轴交点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">一求，零点只有两个 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = -1$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer>，这样就把积分区间缩小到了 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(-1,0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">之后就好做了</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>3.根据题目所给条件的意义划分积分区间</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">比如积分区间是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer>，被积函数在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,c]$</math-renderer> 上大于 0，在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[c,b]$</math-renderer> 上小于 0，那么自然而然地就想到要划分成这两个区间</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：<a href=\"#328-%E5%AE%9A%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E6%8B%86%E6%88%90%E4%B8%8D%E5%AE%9A%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86\">&gt;&gt; 3.2.8 定积分拆成不定积分</a></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-327-多个定积分比较大小\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#327-多个定积分比较大小\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.2.7 多个定积分比较大小</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.两个定积分相减</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.使用定积分计算技巧，如区间再现等</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>3.使用某个定积分作为中介</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1 = \\int_0^{\\pi /2}{\\cos{(\\sin{t})}dt}, I_2 = \\int_0^{\\pi /2}{\\sin{(\\cos{t})}dt}, I_3 = \\int_0^{\\pi /2}{\\sin{(\\sin{t})}dt}$</math-renderer>，则（）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">A. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1 &amp;gt; I_2 = I_3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">B. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1 = I_2 &amp;gt; I_3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">C. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1 &amp;lt; I_2 = I_3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">D. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_2 &amp;gt; I_1 = I_3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：A</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_3$</math-renderer> 区间再现，即令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t = \\dfrac{\\pi}{2} - x$</math-renderer>，得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_3 = I_2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">再比较 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_3$</math-renderer> 的大小</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t \\in [0,\\dfrac{\\pi}{2}]$</math-renderer> 时，$\\sin{t}$ 单调增加，$\\cos{t}$ 单调减小，所以</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\cos{(\\sin{t})} &amp;gt; \\cos{t}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\sin{(\\sin{t})} &amp;lt; \\sin{t}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由被积函数的大小关系推出积分的大小关系：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1 &amp;gt; \\int_0^{\\pi /2}{\\cos{t}dt} = \\sin{t}\\vert_0^{\\pi /2} = 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_3 &amp;lt; \\int_0^{\\pi /2}{\\sin{t}dt} = -\\cos{t}\\vert_0^{\\pi /2} = 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因此 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1 &amp;gt; 1 &amp;gt; I_3$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-328-定积分拆成不定积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#328-定积分拆成不定积分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.2.8 定积分拆成不定积分</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,1]$</math-renderer> 上可导，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x)&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer>，$F(x) = \\int_0^1{\\lvert f(x)-f(t) \\rvert dt}$，则在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,1]$</math-renderer> 上有（）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">A. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) \\geqslant F(\\dfrac{1}{2})$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">B. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) \\leqslant F(\\dfrac{1}{2})$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">C. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(\\dfrac{1}{2}) \\geqslant F(0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">D. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(1) \\leqslant F(\\dfrac{1}{2})$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：A</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这种选择题是可以设特例进行排除法的，比如设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当然对于正经解法是，$F(x) = \\int_0^1{\\lvert f(x)-f(t) \\rvert dt} = \\int_0^x[f(x)-f(t)]dt + \\int_x^1[f(t) - f(x)]dt$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">之后自然而然地求导，就做出来了</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-33-反常积分审敛法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#33-反常积分审敛法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.3 反常积分审敛法</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：无穷区间上的反常积分：定义 性质 常用结论 判敛法\n无界函数的反常积分：定义 性质 常用结论 判敛法</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-331-比较审敛法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#331-比较审敛法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.3.1 比较审敛法</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于每个瑕点或无限区间都要对区域进行划分</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于无限反常积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer>，$\\int_a^{+\\infty}g(x),\\textrm{d}x$，$f(x),g(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,+\\infty)$</math-renderer> 上连续非负</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0 \\leqslant f(x) \\leqslant g(x), a \\leqslant x &amp;lt; +\\infty$</math-renderer> 时，</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}g(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 收敛，那么 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 也收敛</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 发散，那么 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}g(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 也发散</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于瑕积分类似</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">推论：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于无限反常积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer>，$f(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,+\\infty)$</math-renderer> 上连续非负</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果存在常数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$M&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer> 及 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$p&amp;gt;1$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) \\leqslant \\dfrac{M}{x^p}, a \\leqslant x &amp;lt; +\\infty$</math-renderer>，那么 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 收敛</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果存在常数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$N&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) \\geqslant \\dfrac{N}{x}, a \\leqslant x &amp;lt; +\\infty$</math-renderer>，那么 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 发散</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于瑕积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^b f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer>，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a$</math-renderer> 为瑕点，$f(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(a,b]$</math-renderer> 上连续非负</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果存在常数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$M&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer> 及 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$p&amp;gt;1$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) \\leqslant \\dfrac{M}{(x-a)^p}, a &amp;lt; x \\leqslant b$</math-renderer>，那么 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^b f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 收敛</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果存在常数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$N&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) \\geqslant \\dfrac{N}{x-a}, a &amp;lt; x \\leqslant b$</math-renderer>，那么 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^b f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 发散</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">比较审敛法的极限形式：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于无限反常积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer>，$\\int_a^{+\\infty}g(x),\\textrm{d}x$，$f(x),g(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,+\\infty)$</math-renderer> 上连续非负，$\\lim_{x \\to +\\infty}\\dfrac{f(x)}{g(x)} \\to \\lambda$</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0 &amp;lt; \\lambda &amp;lt; +\\infty$</math-renderer> 时，$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$，$\\int_a^{+\\infty}g(x),\\textrm{d}x$ 具有相同的敛散性</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lambda = 0$</math-renderer> 时，若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}g(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 收敛，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 也收敛</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lambda = +\\infty$</math-renderer> 时，若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}g(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 发散，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer> 也发散</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于瑕积分类似</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-332-极限审敛法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#332-极限审敛法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.3.2 极限审敛法</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于每个瑕点或无限区间都要对区域进行划分</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于无限反常积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^{+\\infty}f(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer>，$f(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,+\\infty)$</math-renderer> 上连续非负</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若存在常数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\rho&amp;gt;1$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{x\\to+\\infty}x^\\rho f(x)=c&amp;lt;+\\infty$</math-renderer>，则积分收敛</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若存在常数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\rho=1$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{x\\to+\\infty}xf(x)=c&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer> 或为$+\\infty$，则积分发散</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于瑕积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(x),\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer>，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a$</math-renderer> 为瑕点，$f(x)$ 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上连续非负</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若存在常数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0&amp;lt;\\rho&amp;lt;1$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{x\\to a^+}(x-a)^\\rho f(x)=c$</math-renderer> 存在，则积分收敛</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若存在常数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\rho=1$</math-renderer>，使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim\\limits_{x\\to a^+}(x-a)f(x)=c&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer> 或为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$+\\infty$</math-renderer>，则积分发散</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-34-反常积分的计算\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#34-反常积分的计算\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.4 反常积分的计算</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-341-直接法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#341-直接法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.4.1 直接法</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">直接用牛顿莱布尼茨公式算，对于反常的那个点求极限</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">需要注意的是，对于反常的那个点求极限时，可能需要让趋于极限的自变量保持一致</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">具体看题吧，我这个描述也不太准确</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$I = \\int_1^2{[\\dfrac{1}{x\\ln^2{x}}-\\dfrac{1}{(x-1)^2}]dx}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$I = \\int_1^2{[\\dfrac{1}{x\\ln^2{x}}-\\dfrac{1}{(x-1)^2}]dx} \\\n= \\int_0^{\\ln{2}}{\\dfrac{1}{t^2}dt} - \\int_1^2{\\dfrac{1}{(x-1)^2}]dx} \\\n= -\\dfrac{1}{t}\\vert_0^{\\ln{2}} + \\dfrac{1}{x-1}\\vert_1^2 \\\n= -\\dfrac{1}{\\ln{2}} + \\dfrac{1}{t}\\vert_{t = 0} + 1 - \\dfrac{1}{x-1}\\vert_{x = 1}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这个时候如果认为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{t}\\vert_{t = 0}$</math-renderer> 能够把自变量的符号变成 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer>，等价于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{x}\\vert_{x = 0}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同时 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$- \\dfrac{1}{x-1}\\vert_{x = 1}$</math-renderer> 自变量代换成 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$- \\dfrac{1}{x}\\vert_{x = 0}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">那么可能就会认为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{t}\\vert_{t = 0} - \\dfrac{1}{x-1}\\vert_{x = 1} = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">实际上这是不对的，在这里，两个函数趋于极限，单个函数的自变量不能随便改写，他是有意义的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">或者说成是趋于某点的路径不同？总之就是不一样的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">实际上，$\\dfrac{1}{t}\\vert_{t = 0}$ 应代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$t = \\ln{x}$</math-renderer> 写成 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{\\ln{x}}\\vert_{x = 1}$</math-renderer>，有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\dfrac{1}{t}\\vert_{t = 0} - \\dfrac{1}{x-1}\\vert_{x = 1} = \\dfrac{1}{\\ln{x}}\\vert_{x = 1} - \\dfrac{1}{x-1}\\vert_{x = 1} \\\n= \\lim_{x \\to 1}(\\dfrac{1}{\\ln{x}} - \\dfrac{1}{x-1}) \\\n= \\lim_{x \\to 1}\\dfrac{x-1-\\ln{x}}{(x-1)\\ln{x}} \\\n= \\dfrac{1}{2}$</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-342-极限审敛法不一定需要待定系数\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#342-极限审敛法不一定需要待定系数\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.4.2 极限审敛法不一定需要待定系数</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">虽然我们都知道要对无限反常积分乘一个 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x^\\rho$</math-renderer>、对瑕积分乘一个 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x-a)^\\rho$</math-renderer> 来判别</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">但是实际上怎么乘是有讲究的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有的时候不需要你对这个 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\rho$</math-renderer> 待定系数</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">（或者是说我其实没有真正理解我要接下来要讲的这题，我以为不用待定系数，实际上待定系数也能做hhh）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">（反正从我个人来说，这题从答案来说很简单，题型也很常见，所以还是值得学习的）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：已知积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^{+\\infty}{\\dfrac{x^m \\arctan{x}}{2+x^n}dx},n \\geqslant 0$</math-renderer> 收敛，则（）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">A. m &gt; -2 且 n - m &gt; 1</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">B. m &gt; 0 且 n - m &gt; 1</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">C. m &gt; 0 且 n - m &lt; 1</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">D. m &gt; -2 且 n - m &lt; 1</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：A</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">注意这里的 m 可能是负数，因此 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 0$</math-renderer> 处有瑕积分，容易被忽略</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^{+\\infty}{\\dfrac{x^m \\arctan{x}}{2+x^n}dx} = \\int_0^{1}{\\dfrac{x^m \\arctan{x}}{2+x^n}dx} + \\int_1^{+\\infty}{\\dfrac{x^m \\arctan{x}}{2+x^n}dx} = I_1 + I_2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1$</math-renderer>，因为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0+} x^(-m-1)\\dfrac{x^m \\arctan{x}}{2+x^n} = \\lim_{x \\to 0+} \\dfrac{1}{2}\\dfrac{\\arctan{x}}{x} = \\dfrac{1}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">根据比较审敛法，$I_1$ 收敛要求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0 &amp;lt; -m-1 &amp;lt; 1$</math-renderer> 即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$-2 &amp;lt; m &amp;lt; -1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_2$</math-renderer>，因为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to +\\infty} x^(n-m)\\dfrac{x^m \\arctan{x}}{2+x^n} = \\lim_{x \\to +\\infty} \\dfrac{x^n\\arctan{x}}{2+x^n} = \\lim_{x \\to +\\infty} \\dfrac{\\arctan{x}}{2} = \\dfrac{\\pi}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">根据比较审敛法，$I_2$ 收敛要求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n-m &amp;gt; 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-343-拆成多个反常积分后先算简单的反常积分的定义域再基于这个定义域考虑其他反常积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#343-拆成多个反常积分后先算简单的反常积分的定义域再基于这个定义域考虑其他反常积分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.4.3 拆成多个反常积分后，先算简单的反常积分的定义域，再基于这个定义域考虑其他反常积分</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">毕竟某个反常积分的收敛域是每个反常积分部分的收敛域的交集</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设积分 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I = \\int_1^{+\\infty}\\dfrac{dx}{x^p\\ln^q{x}},p&amp;gt;0,q&amp;gt;0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">易知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = 1$</math-renderer> 为瑕点，于是有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I = \\int_1^c \\dfrac{dx}{x^p\\ln^q{x}} + \\int_c^{+\\infty}\\dfrac{dx}{x^p\\ln^q{x}}  = I_1 + I_2, 1&amp;lt;c&amp;lt;+\\infty$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1$</math-renderer>，观察 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 1}\\dfrac{1}{x^p\\ln^q{x}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">易知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x^p = 1$</math-renderer> 可以化简掉，那么只需要观察 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 1}\\dfrac{1}{\\ln^q{x}}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">泰勒展开 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\ln{x} = 0 + x-1 + o(x-1)$</math-renderer>，所以只需要乘上一个 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x-1)^q$</math-renderer> 就可以得到 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 1}\\dfrac{(x-1)^q}{\\ln^q{x}} = 1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">根据极限审敛法，$0&lt;q&lt;1$ 时 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_1$</math-renderer> 收敛</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">那么之后研究 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I_2$</math-renderer> 时以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0&amp;lt;q&amp;lt;1$</math-renderer> 为前提</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0&amp;lt;q&amp;lt;1,p=1$</math-renderer> 时，$\\int_c^{+\\infty}\\dfrac{dx}{x^p\\ln^q{x}} = \\int_c^{+\\infty}\\dfrac{dx}{x\\ln^q{x}} = \\int_{\\ln{c}}^{+\\infty}\\dfrac{dt}{t^q},t = \\ln{x} = \\dfrac{1}{1-q}t^{1-q}\\vert_{\\ln{c}}^{+\\infty} = +\\infty$，$I_2$ 发散</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0&amp;lt;q&amp;lt;1,p&amp;lt;1$</math-renderer> 时，$\\dfrac{dx}{x^p\\ln^q{x}} \\geqslant \\dfrac{dx}{x\\ln^q{x}}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_c^{+\\infty}\\dfrac{dx}{x\\ln^q{x}}$</math-renderer> 发散，根据比较审敛法，$I_2$ 发散</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0&amp;lt;q&amp;lt;1,p&amp;gt;1$</math-renderer> 时，$\\dfrac{dx}{x^p\\ln^q{x}} \\leqslant \\dfrac{dx}{x^p}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_c^{+\\infty}\\dfrac{dx}{x^p}$</math-renderer> 收敛，根据比较审敛法，$I_2$ 收敛</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">综上，当 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0&amp;lt;q&amp;lt;1,p&amp;gt;1$</math-renderer> 时，原积分收敛</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-35-定积分的几何应用\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#35-定积分的几何应用\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.5 定积分的几何应用</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：平面图形的计算 旋转体的计算 其他应用</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-351-弧长\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#351-弧长\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.5.1 弧长</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$s = \\int_{\\alpha}^{\\beta}{\\sqrt{{x'}^2(t)+{y'}^2(t)}dt}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$s = \\int_{a}^{b}{\\sqrt{1+{y'}^2(x)}dx}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$s = \\int_{\\alpha}^{\\beta}{\\sqrt{{r}^2(\\theta)+{r'}^2(\\theta)}d\\theta}$</math-renderer></p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">特别得，对于极坐标，如果 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x,y$</math-renderer> 可以表达成 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r$</math-renderer> 或者 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\theta$</math-renderer> 的函数，那么也可以把 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r$</math-renderer> 或者 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\theta$</math-renderer> 视为参数，有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$s = \\int_{\\alpha}^{\\beta}{\\sqrt{{x'}^2(r)+{y'}^2(r)}dr}$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-352-体积\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#352-体积\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.5.2 体积</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = y(x)$</math-renderer> 与 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a, x = b$</math-renderer>，$x$ 轴围成的曲边梯形绕 x 轴旋转一周所成的旋转体体积</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$V = \\pi\\int_a^b{y^2(x)dx},a&amp;lt;b$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = y_2(x), y = y_1(x), x = a, x = b(y_2(x) \\geqslant y_1(x) \\geqslant 0)$</math-renderer> 围成的图形绕 x 轴旋转一周所成的旋转体体积</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$V = \\pi\\int_a^b{[y_2^2(x)-y_1^2(x)]dx},a&amp;lt;b$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = y_2(x), y = y_1(x), x = a, x = b(b \\geqslant a \\geqslant 0,y_2(x) \\geqslant y_1(x) \\geqslant 0)$</math-renderer> 围成的图形绕 y 轴旋转一周所成的旋转体体积</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$V = 2\\pi\\int_a^b{x(y_2(x)-y_1(x))dx}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-353-面积\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#353-面积\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.5.3 面积</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上的曲线 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=f(x)$</math-renderer> 的弧段绕 x 轴旋转一周所成的旋转曲面的面积</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$S = 2\\pi\\int_a^b \\lvert y \\rvert ds$</math-renderer></p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-36-由积分定义的函数\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#36-由积分定义的函数\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.6 由积分定义的函数</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上非负连续，严格单增，且存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_n \\in [a,b]$</math-renderer> 使得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[f(x_n)]^n = \\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\int_a^b{[f(x)]^n}dx$</math-renderer>，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}{x_n}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上非负连续，严格单增</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\int_a^b{[f(x)]^n}dx &amp;lt; \\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\int_a^b{[f(b)]^n}dx = f^n(b)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">放缩：$\\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\int_{b-\\frac{1}{n}}^b{[f(x)]^n}dx &lt; \\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\int_a^b{[f(x)]^n}dx$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由积分中值定理，$\\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\int_{b-\\frac{1}{n}}^b{[f(x)]^n}dx = \\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\dfrac{1}{n}f^n(\\xi_n),b-\\dfrac{1}{n}&lt;\\xi_n&lt;b$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\dfrac{1}{n}f^n(\\xi_n) &amp;lt; \\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\int_a^b{[f(x)]^n}dx &amp;lt; f^n(b)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{b-a}\\dfrac{1}{n}f^n(\\xi_n) &amp;lt; [f(x_n)]^n &amp;lt; f^n(b)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{\\sqrt[n]{n(b-a)}}f(\\xi_n) &amp;lt; f(x_n) &amp;lt; f(b)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由极限的保号性得：$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}\\dfrac{1}{\\sqrt[n]{n(b-a)}}f(\\xi_n) &lt; \\lim_{n \\to \\infty}f(x_n) &lt; f(b)$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$b-\\dfrac{1}{n}&amp;lt;\\xi_n&amp;lt;b$</math-renderer>，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}\\dfrac{1}{\\sqrt[n]{n(b-a)}} = 1, \\lim_{n \\to \\infty}f(\\xi_n) = f(b)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(b) &amp;lt; \\lim_{n \\to \\infty}f(x_n) &amp;lt; f(b)$</math-renderer> 夹逼得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{n \\to \\infty}x_n = b$</math-renderer></p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-37-积分不等式的证明\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#37-积分不等式的证明\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.7 积分不等式的证明</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：变限积分函数 积分不等式 零点问题</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-371-视为变限函数\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#371-视为变限函数\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.7.1 视为变限函数</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设要证某式 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$&amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer>（或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\geqslant 0$</math-renderer>）的形式，可将一边看成变限函数，用微分学的办法证明</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如单调性，最值，拉格朗日中值定理，拉格朗日余项的泰勒公式等</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-372-利用积分性质\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#372-利用积分性质\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.7.2 利用积分性质</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设要证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(x)dx \\geqslant \\int_a^bg(x)dx, a &amp;lt; x &amp;lt; b$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">先证在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) \\geqslant g(x)$</math-renderer>，则根据积分的性质自然有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(x)dx \\geqslant \\int_a^bg(x)dx, a &amp;lt; x &amp;lt; b$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设要证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(x)dx &amp;gt; \\int_a^bg(x)dx, a &amp;lt; x &amp;lt; b$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">先证在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x), g(x)$</math-renderer> 连续，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) \\geqslant g(x)$</math-renderer>，并且至少存在一点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_1 \\in [a,b]$</math-renderer> 使 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x_1) &amp;gt; g(x_1)$</math-renderer>，则由积分的性质有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(x)dx &amp;gt; \\int_a^bg(x)dx, a &amp;lt; x &amp;lt; b$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">此外，还有：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">积分中值定理，积分变量代换，分部积分等</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果一个式子有积分号，一个没有积分号，要比较它们的大小，可以统一化为没有积分号或者统一有积分号</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果区间不一致，化为区间一致</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-373-零点问题\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#373-零点问题\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.7.3 零点问题</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">化成变限积分</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用积分中值定理</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上存在二阶导数，试证明：存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi, \\eta \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer>，使</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">(1) <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(t)dt = f(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(b-a)+\\dfrac{1}{24}f''(\\xi)(b-a)^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">(2) <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_a^bf(t)dt = \\dfrac{1}{2}(f(a)+f(b))(b-a)-\\dfrac{1}{12}f''(\\eta)(b-a)^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证明：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">法 1</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">(1) 化成变限积分：令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(x) = \\int_{x_0}^xf(t)dt$</math-renderer>，将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(x)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x =x_0$</math-renderer> 处展开成泰勒公式至 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n=2$</math-renderer>，有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(x) = \\varphi(x_0)+\\varphi'(x_0)(x-x_0)+\\dfrac{1}{2}\\varphi''(x_0)(x-x_0)^2+\\dfrac{1}{3!}\\varphi'''(\\xi)(x-x_0)^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(x_0) = 0, \\varphi'(x_0) = f(x_0), \\varphi''(x_0) = f'(x_0), \\varphi'''(\\xi) = f''(\\xi)$</math-renderer>，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\in (x_0,x)$</math-renderer> 或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi \\in (x,x_0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\varphi(x) = \\int_{x_0}^xf(t)dt$</math-renderer> 代入得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{x_0}^xf(t)dt = f(x_0)(x-x_0)+\\dfrac{1}{2}f'(x_0)(x-x_0)^2+\\dfrac{1}{6}f''(\\xi)(x-x_0)^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若两点都是导数信息或函数信息，则对两点分别展开：对照欲证的式子，令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0 = \\dfrac{a+b}{2}$</math-renderer>，再分别以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = a, x = b$</math-renderer> 代入，得：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{\\frac{a+b}{2}}^af(t)dt = f(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(\\dfrac{a-b}{2})+\\dfrac{1}{2}f'(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(\\dfrac{a-b}{2})^2+\\dfrac{1}{6}f''(\\xi_1)(\\dfrac{a-b}{2})^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{\\frac{a+b}{2}}^bf(t)dt = f(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(\\dfrac{b-a}{2})+\\dfrac{1}{2}f'(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(\\dfrac{b-a}{2})^2+\\dfrac{1}{6}f''(\\xi_2)(\\dfrac{b-a}{2})^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第二个式子 - 第一个式子，得：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\int_{a}^bf(t)dt = f(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(b-a)+\\dfrac{1}{48}<a href=\"b-a\">f''(\\xi_1)+f''(\\xi_2)</a>^3$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">显然，接下来要证明存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_3 = \\dfrac{1}{2}[f''(\\xi_1)+f''(\\xi_2)]$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_1,\\xi_2,\\xi_3 \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">题目没给二阶导连续，但是我不知道除了连续函数的介值定理之外还能怎么证</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">(2) 因为待证式中出现的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a), f(b)$</math-renderer> 很明显是需要令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0 = a, b$</math-renderer>，那么为了化简，剩下的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 只能是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = \\dfrac{a+b}{2}$</math-renderer>，所以先尝试用老方法：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{a}^{\\frac{a+b}{2}}f(t)dt = f(a)(\\dfrac{b-a}{2})+\\dfrac{1}{2}f'(a)(\\dfrac{b-a}{2})^2+\\dfrac{1}{6}f''(\\xi_1)(\\dfrac{b-a}{2})^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{b}^{\\frac{a+b}{2}}f(t)dt = f(b)(\\dfrac{a-b}{2})+\\dfrac{1}{2}f'(b)(\\dfrac{a-b}{2})^2+\\dfrac{1}{6}f''(\\xi_2)(\\dfrac{a-b}{2})^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第一个式子 - 第二个式子，得：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\int_a^b{f(t)dt} = <a href=\"%5Cdfrac%7Bb-a%7D%7B2%7D\">f(a) + f(b)</a>+\\dfrac{1}{2}<a href=\"%5Cdfrac%7Bb-a%7D%7B2%7D\">f'(a)-f'(b)</a>^2+\\dfrac{1}{48}<a href=\"b-a\">f''(\\xi_1)+f''(\\xi_2)</a>^3$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对比题目，要证 $\\dfrac{1}{8}<a href=\"b-a\">f'(a)-f'(b)</a>^2+\\dfrac{1}{48}<a href=\"b-a\">f''(\\xi_1)+f''(\\xi_2)</a>^3 = -\\dfrac{1}{12}f''(\\eta)(b-a)^3$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">为了凑二阶导，对 $\\dfrac{1}{8}<a href=\"b-a\">f'(a)-f'(b)</a>^2$ 使用中值定理，得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\dfrac{1}{8}<a href=\"b-a\">f'(a)-f'(b)</a>^2 = -\\dfrac{1}{8}f''(\\xi_3)(b-a)^3$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">${-\\dfrac{1}{8}f''(\\xi_3)+\\dfrac{1}{48}[f''(\\xi_1)+f''(\\xi_2)]} = -\\dfrac{1}{12}f''(\\eta)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">${-\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\xi_3)+\\dfrac{1}{12}[f''(\\xi_1)+f''(\\xi_2)]} = -\\dfrac{1}{3}f''(\\eta)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_4 = \\dfrac{1}{2}[f''(\\xi_1)+f''(\\xi_2)]$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即证 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$-\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\xi_3)+\\dfrac{1}{6}f''(\\xi_4) = -\\dfrac{1}{3}f''(\\eta)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_1,\\xi_2,\\xi_3,\\xi_4,\\eta \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">接下来如果用连续函数介值定理的话自然很好证……但是这仍然是不行的……</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">法 2：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">书本上的第二小问的答案：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">(2) 用常数 k 值法</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\int_a^bf(t)dt-\\dfrac{1}{2}(f(a)+f(b))(b-a)}{(b-a)^3} = K$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">作函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) = \\int_a^x{f(t)dt}-\\dfrac{1}{2}(f(x)+f(a))(x-a)-K(x-a)^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(a) = F(b) = 0$</math-renderer>，所以存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\eta_1 \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 使 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F'(\\eta_1) = 0$</math-renderer>，即</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(\\eta_1)-\\dfrac{1}{2}f'(\\eta_1)(\\eta_1-a)-\\dfrac{1}{2}(f(\\eta_1)+f(a))-3K(\\eta_1-a)^2 = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">化简为</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(\\eta_1)-f(a)-f'(\\eta_1)(\\eta_1-a)-6K(\\eta_1-a)^2 = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又由泰勒公式有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(a) = f(\\eta_1) + f'(\\eta_1)(a-\\eta_1) + \\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\eta)(a-\\eta_1)^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">联立上述二式，得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$-6K = \\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\eta)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(\\eta) = -12K$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(\\eta) = -12\\dfrac{\\int_a^bf(t)dt-\\dfrac{1}{2}(f(a)+f(b))(b-a)}{(b-a)^3}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">原式得证</p>\n<p
