dir=\"auto\">这个书本的第二小问的答案倒是很靠谱</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">或许可以参考这个答案做第一小问</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">(1) 用常数 k 值法</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\int_a^bf(t)dt-\\dfrac{1}{2}(f(\\dfrac{a+b}{2}))(b-a)}{(b-a)^3} = K$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">作函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) = \\int_a^x{f(t)dt}-\\dfrac{1}{2}f(\\dfrac{x+a}{2})(x-a)-K(x-a)^3$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(a) = F(b) = 0$</math-renderer>，所以存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\xi_1 \\in (a,b)$</math-renderer> 使 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F'(\\xi_1) = 0$</math-renderer>，即</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(\\xi_1) - \\dfrac{1}{4}f'(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2})(\\xi_1 - a) - \\dfrac{1}{2}f(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2})  - 3K(\\xi_1-a)^2 = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又由泰勒公式有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(\\xi_1) = f(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2}) + f'(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2})(\\dfrac{\\xi_1-a}{2}) + \\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\xi_2)(\\dfrac{\\xi_1-a}{2})^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">联立上述二式，得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2}) + f'(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2})(\\dfrac{\\xi_1-a}{2}) + \\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\xi_2)(\\dfrac{\\xi_1-a}{2})^2 - \\dfrac{1}{4}f'(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2})(\\xi_1 - a) - \\dfrac{1}{2}f(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2})  - 3K(\\xi_1-a)^2 = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">化简得：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{1}{2}f(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2}) - \\dfrac{1}{4}f'(\\dfrac{\\xi_1+a}{2})(\\xi_1 - a) + (\\dfrac{1}{16}f''(\\xi_2)-3K)(\\xi_1-a)^2 = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">之后感觉做不下去，可能是我哪错了</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">法 3：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">(1)</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">泰勒展开</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = f(x_0)+f'(x_0)(x-x_0)+\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\xi)(x-x_0)^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">只令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0 = \\dfrac{a+b}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = f(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})+f'(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(x-\\dfrac{a+b}{2})+\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\xi)(x-\\dfrac{a+b}{2})^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">两边在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 上积分</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\int_a^bf(x)dx = \\int_a^bf(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})dx+\\int_a^bf'(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(x-\\dfrac{a+b}{2})dx+\\int_a^b\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\xi)(x-\\dfrac{a+b}{2})^2dx \\\n= f(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(b-a)+f'(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})[\\dfrac{1}{2}(x-\\dfrac{a+b}{2})^2]\\vert_a^b+\\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\xi)[\\dfrac{1}{3}(x-\\dfrac{a+b}{2})^3]\\vert_a^b \\\n= f(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(b-a)+f'(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})\\dfrac{1}{2}[(\\dfrac{b-a}{2})^2-(\\dfrac{a-b}{2})^2] + \\dfrac{1}{2}f''(\\xi)\\dfrac{1}{3}[(\\dfrac{b-a}{2})^3-(\\dfrac{a-b}{2})^3] \\\n= f(\\dfrac{a+b}{2})(b-a) + 0 + \\dfrac{1}{24}f''(\\xi)(b-a)^3$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x_0$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[a,b]$</math-renderer> 的中心上才有这样的效果</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-374-一重积分转化为二重积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#374-一重积分转化为二重积分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.7.4 一重积分转化为二重积分</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">一般是多个对 x 积分的一重积分的乘积</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">可以设为对 x 积分和对 y 积分的一重积分的乘积，进而化为对 x 和 y 的二重积分</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">注意这个二重积分的计算可能需要 x 和 y 的对换</p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,1]$</math-renderer> 上的单调增加的连续函数，证明：$\\dfrac{\\int_0^1{xf^3(x)dx}}{\\int_0^1{xf^2(x)dx}} \\geqslant \\dfrac{\\int_0^1{f^3(x)dx}}{\\int_0^1{f^2(x)dx}}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">变形：$\\int_0^1{xf^3(x)dx}\\int_0^1{f^2(x)dx} \\geqslant \\int_0^1{f^3(x)dx}\\int_0^1{xf^2(x)dx}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">为了转化为二重积分，区分自变量：$\\int_0^1{xf^3(x)dx}\\int_0^1{f^2(y)dy} \\geqslant \\int_0^1{f^3(x)dx}\\int_0^1{yf^2(y)dy}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">转化为二重积分：$\\iint_D{xf^3(x)f^2(y)dxdy} \\geqslant \\iint_D{f^3(x)yf^2(y)dxdy}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即证：$\\iint_D{(x-y)f^3(x)f^2(y)dxdy} \\geqslant 0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">取 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I = \\iint_D{(x-y)f^3(x)f^2(y)dxdy}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同理，在区分自变量时将 x 和 y 对换，相当于对于 I 的 x 和 y 对换，I 不变：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I = \\iint_D{(y-x)f^3(y)f^2(x)dxdy}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">两式相加，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$2I = \\iint_D{f^2(x)f^2(y)[(x-y)f(x)+(y-x)f(y)]dxdy} = \\iint_D{f^2(x)f^2(y)(y-x)[f(y) - f(x)]dxdy}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">又因为单调性，有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(y-x)[f(y) - f(x) \\geqslant 0$</math-renderer> 对任意 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x,y \\in [0,1]$</math-renderer> 成立</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$2I \\geqslant 0$</math-renderer> 即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I \\geqslant 0$</math-renderer> 得证，即原不等式得证</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-38-常用结论\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#38-常用结论\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.8 常用结论</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-381-函数比值极限与积分比值之间的关系\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#381-函数比值极限与积分比值之间的关系\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.8.1 函数比值极限与积分比值之间的关系</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$g(x)$</math-renderer> 在 x = 0 的某邻域内连续，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to 0} \\dfrac{f(x)}{g(x)} = 1$</math-renderer>，则</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int^x_0{f(t)}dt \\sim \\int^x_0{g(t)}dt$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-382-奇偶性周期性\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#382-奇偶性周期性\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.8.2 奇偶性、周期性</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">被积函数关于积分区间偶对称，区间减半，积分乘 2</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">被积函数关于积分区间奇对称，积分 = 0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">被积函数为周期函数，积分区间可以根据周期化简</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-383-华里士公式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#383-华里士公式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.8.3 华里士公式</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">华里士公式（根据区间再现公式可知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}\\sin^nx,\\textrm{d}x=\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}\\cos^nx,\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer>）：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}\\sin^nx,\\textrm{d}x=\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}\\cos^nx,\\textrm{d}x=\\left{\\begin{array}{ll}\n\\dfrac{n-1}{n}\\cdot\\dfrac{n-3}{n-2}\\cdot\\cdots\\cdot\\dfrac{2}{3}\\cdot1, &amp; n = 2k+1, k = 1,2... \\\n\\dfrac{n-1}{n}\\cdot\\dfrac{n-3}{n-2}\\cdot\\cdots\\cdot\\dfrac{1}{2}\\cdot\\dfrac{\\pi}{2}, &amp; n = 2k, k = 1,2...\n\\end{array}\\right.$</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^\\pi\\sin^nx,\\textrm{d}x=2\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}\\sin^nx,\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\int_0^\\pi\\cos^nx,\\textrm{d}x=\\left{\\begin{array}{lcl}\n0, &amp; &amp; n = 2k+1, k = 0,1,2... \\\n2\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}\\cos^nx,\\textrm{d}x, &amp; &amp; n = 2k, k = 1,2...\n\\end{array}\\right.$</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\int_0^{2\\pi}\\sin^nx,\\textrm{d}x=\\int_0^{2\\pi}\\cos^nx,\\textrm{d}x=\\left{\\begin{array}{lcl}\n0, &amp; &amp; n = 2k+1, k = 0,1,2... \\\n4\\int_0^\\frac{\\pi}{2}\\sin^nx,\\textrm{d}x, &amp; &amp; n = 2k, k = 1,2...\n\\end{array}\\right.$</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-384-伽马公式\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#384-伽马公式\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>3.8.4 伽马公式</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">将阶乘化为积分</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^{+\\infty}x^ne^{-x},\\textrm{d}x=n!=\\Gamma(n+1)$</math-renderer>。（$n\\in N^*$）</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{-\\infty}^{+\\infty}e^{-x^2}x^{2n},\\textrm{d}x=\\Gamma\\left(\\dfrac{2n+1}{2}\\right)$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Gamma(x+1)=x\\Gamma(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Gamma(p)\\Gamma(1-p)=\\dfrac{\\pi}{\\sin p\\pi}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n\\to\\infty$</math-renderer>时，$\\Gamma(n+1)=\\sqrt{2\\pi n}\\left(\\dfrac{n}{e}\\right)^n$</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Gamma\\left(\\dfrac{1}{2}\\right)=\\sqrt{\\pi}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-385-常用积分\" \\dfrac{\\sqrt{\\pi}}{2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" href=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/blob/master/AdvMath/ex1.jpg\"><img src=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/raw/master/AdvMath/ex1.jpg\" height=\"200\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"></a></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">多元函数的连续、可微都是用重极限定义的，动点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x,y)$</math-renderer> 沿任意路径趋向 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">多元函数的可导是指一阶偏导数存在，是用一元函数极限定义的，动点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x,y)$</math-renderer> 沿坐标轴趋向 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：考虑二元函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 的下面 4 条性质：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">① <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 处连续</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">② <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 处的两个偏导数连续</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">③ <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 处可微</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">④ <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 处的两个偏导数存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若用“P =&gt; Q”表示可由性质 P 推出性质 Q，则有（）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">A. ② =&gt; ③ =&gt; ①</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">B. ③ =&gt; ② =&gt; ①</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">C. ③ =&gt; ④ =&gt; ①</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">D. ③ =&gt; ① =&gt; ④</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：A</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-412-讨论二重极限\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#412-讨论二重极限\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.1.2 讨论二重极限</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">证明二重极限 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0, y \\to y_0}f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 不存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">取两种不同的路径，极限 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0, y \\to y_0}f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 不相等</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">或取某一路径极限 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0, y \\to y_0}f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 不存在</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求二重极限 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{x \\to x_0, y \\to y_0}f(x,y)$</math-renderer></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用极限的性质（如四则运算法则，夹逼准则）</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">消去分母中极限为零的因子（通常采用有理化，等价无穷小代换等）</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">转化为一元函数极限</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">无穷小*有界量 = 无穷小</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-413-讨论二元函数的连续性偏导数存在性\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#413-讨论二元函数的连续性偏导数存在性\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.1.3 讨论二元函数的连续性、偏导数存在性</h4>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-414-讨论二元函数的可微性\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#414-讨论二元函数的可微性\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.1.4 讨论二元函数的可微性</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用可微的定义</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用可微的必要条件：可微必可导</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即不可导的函数一定不可微</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用可微的充分条件：有连续一阶偏导数的函数一定可微</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">最常用的方法：利用可微的定义。步骤分为：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">考查 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'_x(x_0,y_0),f'_y(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 是否都存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">至少有一个不存在时，不可微</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">都存在时，下一步</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">考查 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{\\Delta x \\to 0, \\Delta y \\to 0}\\dfrac{[f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0+\\Delta y)-f(x_0,y_0)]-[f'_x(x_0,y_0)\\Delta x + f'_y(x_0,y_0)\\Delta y]}{\\rho} = 0,\\rho = \\sqrt{(\\Delta x)^2+(\\Delta y)^2}$</math-renderer> 是否成立</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">不成立则不可微</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">成立则可微</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'_x(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 存在，$f'_y(x,y)$ 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0, y_0)$</math-renderer> 处连续，证明：$f(x,y)$ 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 处可微</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">本题条件比可微的充分条件要弱，所以只能用可微的定义</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第一步，易知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'_x(x_0,y_0),f'_y(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 是否都存在</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">第二步，要考查 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{\\Delta x \\to 0, \\Delta y \\to 0}\\dfrac{[f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0+\\Delta y)-f(x_0,y_0)]-[f'_x(x_0,y_0)\\Delta x + f'_y(x_0,y_0)\\Delta y]}{\\rho} = 0,\\rho = \\sqrt{(\\Delta x)^2+(\\Delta y)^2}$</math-renderer> 是否成立</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Delta z = f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0+\\Delta y)-f(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">加一减一 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Delta z = [f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0+\\Delta y)-f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0)]+[f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0)-f(x_0,y_0)]$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中，由于 $f'<em>y(x,y)$ 在点 $(x_0, y_0)$ 处连续，所以 $\\lim</em>{\\Delta x \\to 0, \\Delta y \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0+\\Delta y)-f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0)}{\\Delta y} = \\lim_{\\Delta x \\to 0, \\Delta y \\to 0}f'_y(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0) = f'_y(x_0,y_0)$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于 $f'<em>x(x_0,y_0)$ 存在，所以 $\\lim</em>{\\Delta x \\to 0, \\Delta y \\to 0}\\dfrac{f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0)-f(x_0,y_0)}{\\Delta x} = f'_x(x_0,y_0)$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">为了方便计算 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Delta z - [f'_x(x_0,y_0)\\Delta x + f'_y(x_0,y_0)\\Delta y]$</math-renderer>，以上二式化为</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0+\\Delta y)-f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0)}{\\Delta y} = f'_y(x_0,y_0) + \\varepsilon_1, \\varepsilon_1 = o(\\Delta x, \\Delta y)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0)-f(x_0,y_0)}{\\Delta x} = f'_x(x_0,y_0) + \\varepsilon_2, \\varepsilon_2 = o(\\Delta x, \\Delta y)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Delta z$</math-renderer> 得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\Delta z = (f'_y(x_0,y_0) + \\varepsilon_1)\\Delta y + (f'_x(x_0,y_0) + \\varepsilon_2)\\Delta x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">待验证式子化为：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\lim_{\\Delta x \\to 0, \\Delta y \\to 0}\\dfrac{[f(x_0+\\Delta x,y_0+\\Delta y)-f(x_0,y_0)]-[f'_x(x_0,y_0)\\Delta x + f'<em>y(x_0,y_0)\\Delta y]}{\\rho} = \\lim</em>{\\Delta x \\to 0, \\Delta y \\to 0}\\dfrac{\\varepsilon_1 \\Delta y + \\varepsilon_2 \\Delta x}{\\rho}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">为了方便放缩，对待验证式子取绝对值，保证各项为正数：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$0 \\leqslant \\dfrac{\\lvert \\varepsilon_1 \\Delta y + \\varepsilon_2 \\Delta x\\rvert}{\\rho} \\leqslant \\dfrac{\\lvert \\varepsilon_1 \\Delta y \\rvert + \\lvert \\varepsilon_2 \\Delta x\\rvert}{\\rho} = \\dfrac{\\lvert \\varepsilon_1 \\rvert \\lvert \\Delta y \\rvert + \\lvert \\varepsilon_2 \\rvert \\lvert \\Delta x\\rvert}{\\rho} \\leqslant \\lvert \\varepsilon_1 \\rvert + \\lvert \\varepsilon_2 \\rvert \\to 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{\\Delta x \\to 0, \\Delta y \\to 0}\\dfrac{\\varepsilon_1 \\Delta y + \\varepsilon_2 \\Delta x}{\\rho} = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 处可微</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-42-二元函数的微分法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#42-二元函数的微分法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.2 二元函数的微分法</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：复合函数的微分法 隐函数的微分法</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-421-全微分形式不变性\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#421-全微分形式不变性\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.2.1 全微分形式不变性</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$z = f(u,v)$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$u = \\varphi(x,y), v = \\psi(x,y)$</math-renderer> 都具有连续一阶偏导数，则复合导数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$z = f[\\varphi(x,y),\\psi(x,y)]$</math-renderer> 可微，且</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$dz = \\dfrac{\\partial z}{\\partial x}dx+\\dfrac{\\partial z}{\\partial y}dy = \\dfrac{\\partial z}{\\partial u}du+\\dfrac{\\partial z}{\\partial v}dv$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-422-隐函数的偏导数与全微分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#422-隐函数的偏导数与全微分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.2.2 隐函数的偏导数与全微分</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由一个方程式确定的隐函数（一元函数）求导法</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x,y)$</math-renderer> 有连续一阶偏导数，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F'_x \\ne 0$</math-renderer>，则由方程 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x,y)=0$</math-renderer> 确定的函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=y(x)$</math-renderer> 可导，且</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{dy}{dx}=-\\dfrac{F'_x}{F'_y}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由一个方程式确定的隐函数（二元函数）求导法</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x,y,z)$</math-renderer> 有连续一阶偏导数，且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F'_z \\ne 0$</math-renderer>，$z = z(x,y)$ 由方程 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x,y,z) = 0$</math-renderer> 所确定，则</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\partial z}{\\partial x} = -\\dfrac{F'_x}{F'_z},\\dfrac{\\partial z}{\\partial y} = -\\dfrac{F'_y}{F'_z}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-423-求复合函数的偏导数与全微分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#423-求复合函数的偏导数与全微分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.2.3 求复合函数的偏导数与全微分</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'_x(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer>，可以先令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = y_0$</math-renderer> 再对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 求导，再令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = x_0$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">当原偏导很难求积分，就再次偏导</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">若函数连续，则利用偏导不变性$\\dfrac{\\partial f}{\\partial x\\partial y}=\\dfrac{\\partial f}{\\partial y\\partial x}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">可以求出参数</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-424-注意是否给出高阶偏导数在某点存在的条件没有则用定义求\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#424-注意是否给出高阶偏导数在某点存在的条件没有则用定义求\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.2.4 注意是否给出高阶偏导数在某点存在的条件，没有则用定义求</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$z = f[\\cos{(x^2+y^2)-1},\\ln{(1+x^2+y^2)}]$</math-renderer>，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f$</math-renderer> 有一阶连续偏导数，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(\\dfrac{\\partial^2{z}}{\\partial{x^2}}-\\dfrac{\\partial^2{z}}{\\partial{x}\\partial{y}}+\\dfrac{\\partial^2{z}}{\\partial{y^2}})\\vert_{(0,0)} = $</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：$4f_z'(0,0)$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">首先由 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f$</math-renderer> 有一阶连续偏导数可得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\partial{z}}{\\partial{x}} = -2x\\sin{(x^2+y^2)}f_1' + \\dfrac{2x}{1+x^2+y^2}f_2'$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\partial{z}}{\\partial{y}} = -2y\\sin{(x^2+y^2)}f_1' + \\dfrac{2y}{1+x^2+y^2}f_2'$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(u,v)$</math-renderer> 没有二阶偏导数存在的条件，故用定义求</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\dfrac{\\partial^2{z}}{\\partial{x^2}} \\vert_{(0,0)} = \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{z_x'(x,0)-z_x'(0,0)}{x} \\\n= \\lim_{x \\to 0}\\dfrac{-2x\\sin{(x^2)}f_1' + \\dfrac{2x}{1+x^2}f_2'}{x} \\\n= 2f_2'(0,0)$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由对称性知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\partial^2{z}}{\\partial{y^2}} \\vert_{(0,0)} = 2f_2'(0,0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\partial^2{z}}{\\partial{x}\\partial{y}} \\vert_{(0,0)} = \\lim_{y \\to 0}\\dfrac{z_x'(0,y)-z_x'(0,0)}{y} = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(\\dfrac{\\partial^2{z}}{\\partial{x^2}}-\\dfrac{\\partial^2{z}}{\\partial{x}\\partial{y}}+\\dfrac{\\partial^2{z}}{\\partial{y^2}})\\vert_{(0,0)} = 4f_2'(0,0)$</math-renderer></p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-43-极值\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#43-极值\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.3 极值</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：无条件极值 条件极值 最值</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-431-驻点与极值点\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#431-驻点与极值点\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.3.1 驻点与极值点</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">驻点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">满足 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'_x(x,y) = f'_y(x,y) = 0$</math-renderer> 的点</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">极值点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">二元函数取极值的必要条件：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$z=f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 一阶偏导数存在且取极值，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f_x'(x_0,y_0)=0$</math-renderer>，$f_y'(x_0,y_0)=0$。三元及以上可以类推</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">二元函数取极值的充分条件：若对函数求二阶偏导 $\\left{\\begin{array}{l}\nf_{xx}''(x_0,y_0)=A \\\nf_{xy}''(x_0,y_0)=B \\\nf_{yy}''(x_0,y_0)=C\n\\end{array}\\right.$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">则 $\\Delta = B^2-AC = \\left{\\begin{array}{l}\n&lt;0\\Rightarrow\\text{极值}\\left{\\begin{array}{l}\nA&lt;0\\Rightarrow\\text{极大值} \\\nA&gt;0\\Rightarrow\\text{极小值}\n\\end{array}\\right.\n\\&gt;0\\Rightarrow\\text{非极值} \\\n=0\\Rightarrow\\text{方法失效，使用定义法}\n\\end{array}\\right.$。只适用于二元函数极值</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-432-二元函数的极值转化为一元函数的极值\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#432-二元函数的极值转化为一元函数的极值\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.3.2 二元函数的极值转化为一元函数的极值</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 在点 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$P_0(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 处有二阶连续偏导数,且 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x,y)$</math-renderer> 在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$P_0$</math-renderer> 取得极大值，则（）</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">A. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f_{xx}''(P_0) \\geqslant 0,f_{yy}''(P_0) \\geqslant 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">B. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f_{xx}''(P_0) &amp;lt; 0,f_{yy}''(P_0) &amp;lt; 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">C. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f_{xx}''(P_0) \\leqslant 0,f_{yy}''(P_0) \\leqslant 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">D. <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f_{xx}''(P_0) \\leqslant 0,f_{yy}''(P_0) \\geqslant 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：C</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) = f(x,y_0)$</math-renderer>，由已知得，$x = x_0$ 是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x)$</math-renderer> 的极大值点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">反证法：若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F''(x_0) &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = x_0$</math-renderer> 是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x)$</math-renderer> 的极小值点，与已知矛盾，故</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F''(x_0) = \\dfrac{d^2}{dx^2}f(x,y_0)\\vert_{x = x_0} = \\dfrac{\\partial^2{f(P_0)}}{\\partial{x^2}} \\leqslant 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同理，令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$G(y) = f(x_0,y)$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = y_0$</math-renderer> 是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$G(y)$</math-renderer> 的极大值点，故</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$G''(x_0) = \\dfrac{d^2}{dy^2}f(x_0,y)\\vert_{y = y_0} = \\dfrac{\\partial^2{f(P_0)}}{\\partial{y^2}} \\leqslant 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">我一开始犯了一个很典型的错误</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">假设 A 成立，此时若 A 的必要条件 B 不成立，则发生矛盾，可证 A 是错误的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">假设 A 成立，此时若推出的条件弱于必要条件 B 时，不能说明 A 就是错的</p>\n</blockquote>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">比如我一开始想，如果 A, C 可以为 0 的话，那么 B^2 - AC 可能 = B^2 &gt;= 0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">此时如果还在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$(x_0,y_0)$</math-renderer> 有极值的话，就需要 B = 0，保证判别式 = 0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这样的话就比这道题中所给的选项强了，或者说这道题中的选项所给的条件就不完善了</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">那么答案是不是就错了呢？不是的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这道题本身正确的解法就是二元函数的极值转化为两个一元函数的极值，然后用反证法</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">反证法的假设，例如：“令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x) = f(x,y_0)$</math-renderer>，若 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F''(x_0) &amp;gt; 0$</math-renderer>，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = x_0$</math-renderer> 是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x)$</math-renderer> 的极小值点”也是没有错的，如果设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F''(x_0) \\geqslant 0$</math-renderer> 那么是不能推出“$x = x_0$ 是 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F(x)$</math-renderer> 的极小值点”的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">反证法本身没有错，反证法的结果也没有错，反证法的结果弱于必要条件，其实也是合理的；</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">如果 A, C 可以为 0，就需要 B = 0，也是没错的。实际上，这是从一个较弱条件变到较强条件的过程，其实……嗯……算是一个推论，但是不能说明原来我的弱条件不对啊</p>\n</blockquote>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-433-多元函数的条件极值\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#433-多元函数的条件极值\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.3.3 多元函数的条件极值</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">步骤：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">构造拉格朗日函数</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求该拉格朗日函数的驻点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解方程组求驻点的方法不统一，需要具体题目具体分析</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<hr>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设三角形三边的长分别为 a, b, c，此三角形的面积设为 S，求此三角形内的点到三边距离乘积的最大值，并求出这三个相应的距离</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：设 P 为三角形内的任意一点，该点到边长分别为 a, b, c 的边的距离分别为 x, y, z，由三角形的面积公式，有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$S = \\dfrac{1}{2}ax + \\dfrac{1}{2}by + \\dfrac{1}{2}cz$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f = xyz$</math-renderer> 在约束 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$ax + by + cz = 2S$</math-renderer> 下的最大值，构造拉格朗日函数：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$w = xyz + \\lambda(ax + by + cz - 2S)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求驻点：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\left{\\begin{array}{l}\n\\dfrac{\\partial w}{\\partial x} = yz + a\\lambda = 0 \\\n\\dfrac{\\partial w}{\\partial y} = xz + b\\lambda = 0 \\\n\\dfrac{\\partial w}{\\partial z} = xy + c\\lambda = 0 \\\n\\dfrac{\\partial w}{\\partial \\lambda} = ax + by + cz - 2S = 0 \\\n\\end{array}\\right.$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由前三个式子算得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{yz}{a} = \\dfrac{xz}{b} = \\dfrac{xy}{c}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">向第四个式子的方向靠拢：$\\dfrac{xyz}{ax} = \\dfrac{xyz}{by} = \\dfrac{xyz}{cz}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">即 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$ax:by:cz = 1:1:1$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$ax + by + cz - 2S = 0$</math-renderer> 有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$3ax = 2S$</math-renderer> =&gt; <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x = \\dfrac{2S}{3a}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">同理，解得：$x = \\dfrac{2S}{3a}, y = \\dfrac{2S}{3b}, z = \\dfrac{2S}{3c}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">点 P 位于三角形边界上时，$f = 0$ 为最小值</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">点 P 位于三角形内部时，$f = \\dfrac{8S^3}{27c}$ 为最大值</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-434-多元函数在有界区域上的最值\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#434-多元函数在有界区域上的最值\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.3.4 多元函数在有界区域上的最值</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">多元函数在有界区域上的最值，或在区域内达到，或在边界上达到</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">在区域内达到时，该店一定是极值点</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">在边界上达到时，属于条件极值问题</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中最大（小）者就是最大（小）值</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-44-二重积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#44-二重积分\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.4 二重积分</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：定义 性质 累次积分 交换积分次序 计算方法</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a dir=\"auto\">更不容易错</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：$I = \\int_{\\pi /4}^{\\pi /2}{d\\theta}\\int_{0}^{1/\\sin{\\theta}}{f(r)rdr} = $</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/blob/master/AdvMath/convert-the-integration-interval.png\"><img src=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/raw/master/AdvMath/convert-the-integration-interval.png\" height=\"475\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_{0}^{1}{dr}\\int_{\\pi /4}^{\\pi /2}{f(r)r d \\theta} + \\int_{1}^{\\sqrt{2}}{dr}\\int_{\\pi /4}^{\\arcsin{1/r}}{f(r)r d \\theta}$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-443-两个定积分的乘积转化成重积分\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#443-两个定积分的乘积转化成重积分\"><svg class=\"octicon \\int_a^b{\\dfrac{1}{f(x)}dx}} = \\int_a^b{f(x)dx · \\int_a^b{\\dfrac{1}{f(y)}dy}} = \\int_a^b{\\dfrac{f(x)}{f(y)}dxdy}$</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-444-极坐标的二重积分化为定积分\" <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 连续，$f(0) = 1$，$F(t) = \\iint_{x^2+y^2 \\leqslant t^2}f(x^2+y^2)dxdy, t \\geqslant 0$，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$F''(0) =$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">要对 t 求两次导，但是被导的函数不是 t 的变限积分，于是就要转化为变限积分</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">于是就转化为先对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\theta$</math-renderer> 积再对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r$</math-renderer> 积：$F(t) = \\int_0^{2\\pi}d\\theta\\int_0^tf(r^2)rdr = 2\\pi\\int_0^tf(r^2)rdr$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">重要的是注意到，对于这种 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(r)$</math-renderer> 函数，先对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\theta$</math-renderer> 积是可以直接积出来的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">我做题的时候已经想到了化成这种形式，但是脑子就是卡壳，没想到先把 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\theta$</math-renderer> 积出来……</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-45-对称性\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#45-对称性\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = x^3, x = -1, y = 1$</math-renderer> 所围成的闭区域，则 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\iint_D {x·\\sin{(x^4y)}d\\sigma} = $</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">答案：0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/blob/master/AdvMath/symmetric.jpg\"><img src=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/raw/master/AdvMath/symmetric.jpg\" height=\"200\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"></a></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.5.2 积分区域关于 y = x 对称</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">积分区域 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$D_1,D_2$</math-renderer> 关于 y = x 对称时，有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\iint_{D_1}{f(x,y)}d\\sigma = \\iint_{D_2}{f(y,x)}d\\sigma$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 在区间 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$[0,1]$</math-renderer> 上连续，并设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^1{f(x)dx} = A$</math-renderer>，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\int_0^1dx\\int_x^1{f(x)f(y)dy}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/blob/master/AdvMath/symmetric_xy.jpg\"><img src=\"/CheapMeow/Math302/raw/master/AdvMath/symmetric_xy.jpg\" height=\"200\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"></a></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I$</math-renderer> 为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$D_1$</math-renderer> 上的积分，由于积分区域关于 y = x 对称，所以对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$D_1$</math-renderer> 积分和对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$D_2$</math-renderer> 积分的值是相同的，所以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$2I = \\int_0^1dy\\int_0^1f(x)f(y)dx = \\int_0^1Af(y)dy = A^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$I = \\dfrac{1}{2}A^2$</math-renderer></p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-46-常用结论\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#46-常用结论\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>4.6 常用结论</h3>\n<h2 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-第五章-常微分方程\" 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>第五章 常微分方程</h2>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a dir=\"auto\">提要：可分离变量方程 齐次方程 一阶线性方程</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-511-可分离变量的微分方程\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#511-可分离变量的微分方程\"><svg class=\"octicon 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.1.1 可分离变量的微分方程</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.定义</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">形如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y'=f(x)g(y)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">可以变型为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}y}{g(y)}=f(x)\\textrm{d}x$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.变形</strong></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">多项式换元</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">形如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}y}{\\textrm{d}x}=f(ax+by+c)$</math-renderer>，其中 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$a,b,c$</math-renderer> 全不为 0</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$u=ax+by+c$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-512-齐次方程\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#512-齐次方程\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.1.2 齐次方程</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.定义</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">形如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}y}{\\textrm{d}x}=\\varphi\\left(\\dfrac{y}{x}\\right)$</math-renderer> 或 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}x}{\\textrm{d}y}=\\varphi\\left(\\dfrac{x}{y}\\right)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$u=\\dfrac{y}{x}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.变形</strong></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}y}{\\textrm{d}x}=\\dfrac{A_1x+B_1y}{A_2x+B_2y}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">除以 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 得到齐次方程</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}y}{\\textrm{d}x}=\\dfrac{A_1x+B_1y+C_1}{A_2x+B_2y+C_2}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x=X+h$</math-renderer>，$y=Y+k$，解方程转化为第一种情况</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-513-一阶线性方程\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#513-一阶线性方程\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.1.3 一阶线性方程</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">形如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}y}{\\textrm{d}x}+P(x)y=Q(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$Q(x)\\equiv 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">分离变量，解得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=Ce^{-\\int P(x),\\textrm{d}x}$</math-renderer></p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$Q(x)\\neq 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">常数变易法，令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=C(x)e^{-\\int P(x),\\textrm{d}x}$</math-renderer>，代入解得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y=e^{-\\int P(x),\\textrm{d}x}(\\int Q(x)e^{\\int P(x),\\textrm{d}x},\\textrm{d}x+C)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">不用记公式，记怎么设的 y，之后只需要代入</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-514-伯努利方程\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#514-伯努利方程\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.定义</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">形如 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}y}{\\textrm{d}x}+P(x)y=Q(x)y^n$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y^{1-n}=z$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>2.变形</strong></p>\n<p data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y^{-n}\\dfrac{\\textrm{d}y}{\\textrm{d}x}+P(x)y^{1-n}=Q(x)$</math-renderer>、</p>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-52-高阶微分方程\" 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.2 高阶微分方程</h3>\n<p dir=\"auto\">提要：可降阶的微分方程 线性方程解的结构定理 线性常系数齐次微分方程 线性常系数非齐次微分方程</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-521-可降阶的高阶微分方程\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#521-可降阶的高阶微分方程\"><svg class=\"octicon 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.2.1 可降阶的高阶微分方程</h4>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y^{(n)}=f(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">连续积分</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y''=f(x,y')$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y'=p$</math-renderer>，$y''=p'$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">视 p 为关于 x 的函数</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y''=f(y,y')$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y'=p$</math-renderer>，$y''=p'$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">视 p 是关于 y 的函数</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-522-线性常系数齐次微分方程\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#522-线性常系数齐次微分方程\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1
