0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.2.2 线性常系数齐次微分方程</h4>\n<table>\n<thead>\n<tr>\n<th align=\"center\">\n<math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r^2+pr+q=0$</math-renderer> 的两个根 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r_1,r_2$</math-renderer>\n</th>\n<th align=\"center\">\n<math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y''+py'+qy=0$</math-renderer> 的通解</th>\n</tr>\n</thead>\n<tbody>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">实根 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r_1 \\ne r_2$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = C_1 e^{r_1 x} + C_2 e^{r_2 x}$</math-renderer></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">实根 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r_1 = r_2$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = (C_1 + C_2 x) e^{r_1 x}$</math-renderer></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">共轭复根 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r_{1,2} \\ne \\alpha \\pm i \\beta$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = e^{\\alpha x}(C_1 \\cos{\\beta x}+C_2 \\sin{\\beta x})$</math-renderer></td>\n</tr>\n</tbody>\n</table>\n<p dir=\"auto\">以此类推</p>\n<table>\n<thead>\n<tr>\n<th align=\"center\">特征方程的根</th>\n<th align=\"center\">微分方程的通解</th>\n</tr>\n</thead>\n<tbody>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">单实根 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$r$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n<td align=\"center\">一项 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$C e^{rx}$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = (C_1 + C_2 x + C_{k}x^{k-1}) e^{r x}$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td x})$</math-renderer>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td align=\"center\">k 重共轭复根 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.2.3 线性常系数非齐次微分方程</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$P_n(x)$</math-renderer>，$P_m(x)$ 分别为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer> 的 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$n$</math-renderer> 次、$m$ 次多项式</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)=P_n(x)e^{\\alpha x}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">特解设为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y^*=e^{\\alpha x}Q_n(x)x^k$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中 k 是特征根 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\alpha$</math-renderer> 的重数，$Q_n(x)$ 系数待定</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)=e^{\\alpha x}[P_m(x)\\cos\\beta x+P_n(x)\\sin\\beta x]$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">特解设为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y^*=e^{\\alpha x}[Q_l^{(1)}(x)\\cos\\beta x+Q_l^{(2)}(x)\\sin\\beta x]x^k$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其中 k 是特征根 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\alpha \\pm i \\beta$</math-renderer> 的重数，$Q_l^{(1)}(x), Q_l^{(2)}(x)$ 的系数待定，$l=\\max{m,n}$</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-53-代换变形构造的更多方法\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#53-代换变形构造的更多方法\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.3 代换、变形、构造的更多方法</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-531-自变量对换\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#531-自变量对换\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.3.1 自变量对换</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">或者说把 y 设为自变量</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求微分方程 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{dy}{dx} = \\dfrac{y}{x+y^4}$</math-renderer> 的通解</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">乍一看上去像是要有一个比值关系，比如令 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$u=\\dfrac{y}{x}$</math-renderer>？但是又不能表达成 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(\\dfrac{y}{x})$</math-renderer> 的形式</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这个时候我老是想着会不会有一种方法化成齐次方程……其实不必，因为只要把 y 看成自变量，比式一变，就变成了一阶非齐次方程 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{dx}{dy} = \\dfrac{x+y^4}{y} = \\dfrac{x}{y} + y^3$</math-renderer>，用常数变易法就好了</p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-532-对题设条件恒等变形利用导数定义构造可分离变量的微分方程\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#532-对题设条件恒等变形利用导数定义构造可分离变量的微分方程\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.3.2 对题设条件恒等变形，利用导数定义构造可分离变量的微分方程</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：设函数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer> 连续，且满足 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x+y) = \\dfrac{f(x)+f(y)}{1-f(x)f(y)}$</math-renderer>，又因 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(0)$</math-renderer> 存在，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">思路：</p>\n<ol dir=\"auto\">\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">求出隐含条件</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对题设条件恒等变形</p>\n</li>\n<li>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用导数定义构造可分离变量的微分方程</p>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">由 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x+y)$</math-renderer> 分母知，$1-f(x)f(y) = 0$ 时，$f(x+y)$ 无定义</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">设存在 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$x$</math-renderer>，使 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)f(y) \\ne 0$</math-renderer>，有题设方程成立</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">此时代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = 0$</math-renderer>，有 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = \\dfrac{f(x)+f(0)}{1-f(x)f(0)}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">变形得：$f(0)[1+f^2(x)] = 0$ 易得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(0) = 0$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">利用导数定义：取 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{f(x+y)-f(y)}{x}$</math-renderer>，其中对于 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x+y)$</math-renderer>，代入题设方程，有</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">$\\dfrac{f(x+y)-f(y)}{x} = \\dfrac{\\dfrac{f(x)+f(y)}{1-f(x)f(y)}-f(y)}{x} \\\n= \\dfrac{f(y)[1+f^2(x)]}{y[1-f(x)f(y)]} \\\n= \\dfrac{f(y)-f(0)}{y}\\dfrac{1+f^2(x)}{1-f(x)f(y)}$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对等式两边取 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\lim_{y \\to 0}$</math-renderer>，得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x) = f'(0)[1+f^2(x)]$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对这个可分离变量的微分方程求解得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x) = \\tan{[f'(0)x]}$</math-renderer></p>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-533-xy-代换\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#533-xy-代换\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.3.3 xy 代换</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：求微分方程 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$xy' = y(\\ln{xy}-1)$</math-renderer> 的通解</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">解：观察到 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$xy'+y$</math-renderer> 和 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$xy$</math-renderer> 所以想到将 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$xy$</math-renderer> 作为新变量，代换之后得</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{du}{dx} = \\dfrac{u}{x}\\ln{u}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">分离变量：$\\dfrac{1}{u\\ln{u}}du = \\dfrac{1}{x}dx$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">两边积分得：$\\ln{\\ln{u}} = \\ln{x} + C_1$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">两边取指数：$\\ln{u} = C_1 x$ 再次取指数 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$u = e^{C_1 x}$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$u = xy$</math-renderer> 得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$y = \\dfrac{1}{x}e^{C_1 x}$</math-renderer></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">遇到非常规的微分方程，那就是一定要变形成见过的</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">因此这个时候就要用一种想法是知道要代换。如果没有想法，那就尝试从整体来看</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">（当然这也算一种马后炮了吧hhh</p>\n</blockquote>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-534-fx---f-x\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#534-fx---f-x\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.3.4 f'(x) = -f(-x)</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\">我知道这个标题很烂……但是我做题的时候确实就是没想到；现在知道了，也确实不知道怎么总结这个东西</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：已知 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x) = -f(-x)$</math-renderer>，求 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x) = -f(-x)$</math-renderer> 代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$-x$</math-renderer> 有：$f'(-x) = -f(x)$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">对 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(x) = -f(-x)$</math-renderer> 两边求导，得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x) = f‘(-x)$</math-renderer>，又代入 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f'(-x) = -f(x)$</math-renderer> 得：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$f''(x) = -f(x)$</math-renderer></p>\n<blockquote>\n<p dir=\"auto\">就是说当同一个函数里面的自变量有的带负号有的不带负号的时候怎么化简：通过求导，把这个关系抬到第二个维度……？真的不会总结了</p>\n</blockquote>\n<h3 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-54-微分方程的应用\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#54-微分方程的应用\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.4 微分方程的应用</h3>\n<h4 tabindex=\"-1\" dir=\"auto\"><a id=\"user-content-541-物理相关\" class=\"anchor\" aria-hidden=\"true\" href=\"#541-物理相关\"><svg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" 2.83Z\"></path></svg></a>5.4.1 物理相关</h4>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><strong>1.注意变化率的正负</strong></p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">例：已知高温物体置于低温物体中，任一时刻，该物体温度对时间的变化率与该时刻物体与介质的温差成正比。现将一初始温度为 120 摄氏度...</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这题在设微分方程的时候，我一开始是设 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{dT}{dt} = k(T-T_0)$</math-renderer>，$T_0$ 为低温物体的温度</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">后面求得 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$T = T_0 + Ce^{kt}$</math-renderer> 我就感觉不对了，因为我下意识地以为 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$Ce^{kt}$</math-renderer> 是单调递增的，所以我就不敢继续求……</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">其实当然是无所谓的，之后代入条件也可以求参，但是为了不让自己怀疑，不如明确参数的物理意义，比如像这样设：</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\"><math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{dT}{dt} = -k(T-T_0)$</math-renderer>，$T_0$ 为低温物体的温度，$k &gt; 0$</p>\n<p dir=\"auto\">这样物理意义就明确表示了 <math-renderer class=\"js-inline-math\" style=\"display: inline\" data-static-url=\"https://github.githubassets.com/static\" data-run-id=\"ecb20d9ab5fb9dc0ec54d4604a155f49\">$\\dfrac{dT}{dt}$</math-renderer> 是负的，说明了高温物体是在降温的</p>\n</article>","renderedFileInfo":null,"tabSize":8,"topBannersInfo":{"overridingGlobalFundingFile":false,"globalPreferredFundingPath":null,"repoOwner":"CheapMeow","repoName":"Math302","showInvalidCitationWarning":false,"citationHelpUrl":"https://docs.github.com/en/github/creating-cloning-and-archiving-repositories/creating-a-repository-on-github/about-citation-files","showDependabotConfigurationBanner":false,"actionsOnboardingTip":null},"truncated":false,"viewable":true,"workflowRedirectUrl":null,"symbols":{"timedOut":false,"notAnalyzed":true,"symbols":[]}},"copilotAccessInfo":{"accessAllowed":false,"hasSubscriptionEnded":false,"orgHasCFBAccess":false,"userHasCFIAccess":false,"userHasOrgs":false,"userIsOrgAdmin":false,"userIsOrgMember":false,"business":null},"csrf_tokens":{"/CheapMeow/Math302/branches":{"post":"CmD_UzFlQHEekQe9ieoW59tuqbhtjfrBkyqldotiYUBeIbyTD-z7Z2UoU5Ez2W5FL6s25OMn9b_nxWdgrn0sMw"}}},"title":"Math302/AdvMath/AdvMath.md
